Is the United States Factually Recognizing Soviet Russia? 47

(Washington) Although the White House denied today that the US President's appeal for a peace guarantee was directly sent to Soviet Russia as an indication of preparing a reply, many in Congress believe this is the first step towards resuming diplomatic relations. Several people even said that if Kalinin, the chairman of the Central Executive Committee of the Soviet Union, also directly replies to the US President, it could be regarded as establishing diplomatic relations in legal terms. Several international law experts also stated that the US President's action already recognizes the Central Executive Committee as the de facto government of the Soviet Union. Senator Robinson, who usually speaks on behalf of the government in the Senate, while refusing to accept this broad meaning, also said that the President's message will definitely have an impact on the recognition issue. Furthermore, Bo, a Republican leader who has always advocated recognizing Soviet Russia, said that this move is a point towards practical clarity.

However, apart from views on legal terminology, officials and most members of Congress believe that the President may not immediately raise the issue of recognition. According to government advisors, if recognition is granted at this time, it may hinder the progress of the World Economic Conference, as several countries, even if they do not consider it an unfriendly act, will deem it impolite. However, it is believed that the President has allowed US representatives in London to freely exchange views with Soviet representatives, just like representatives from other countries. (16th Kuo Min She dispatch)

White House Statement 48

(Washington) People in the White House claimed that the direct delivery of President Roosevelt's appeal for world peace to Soviet Russia does not indicate a current plan for early recognition of Soviet Russia. The President did not think about the issue of recognition when issuing this appeal. However, it must be explained that the US representatives attending the World Economic Conference will freely talk with Soviet representatives, just like representatives from other countries. (16th Kuo Min dispatch)

US Congressman Believes Japan Receives a Head-on Blow 49

Forming a United Front to Deal with Aggressor Nations

(Washington) Both Democrats and Republicans called the declaration a significant and powerful document, but they differed in their interpretation of its intent. Friends of the government claimed that the President's intent was to persuade all countries to abandon political disputes and unite in support of the London Conference, as it is considered the most important international conference ever held.

Congressman Blanton, however, believes that the message is nothing short of a head-on blow to Japan, saying that the President's true intention is to persuade Japan to stop its unjust aggressive war against China. Although Japan is not mentioned in the message, the core of the message is that if armed forces are not sent out of one's own country, they will be publicly recognized as aggressors, which is implicitly directed at Japan. Blanton believes that the President's handling of the Far East situation is often very clever, so he does not believe this statement is directed at belligerent countries in South America.

Many more members of Congress, including Speaker Rayburn, believe that the main target of the message is Germany, as the message was issued when the Disarmament Conference was in a stalemate. However, as Rayburn stated, what the President proposed was to form a united front to deal with those engaged in military actions or those who are likely to engage in military actions, and Germany is certainly among them. The true meaning is self-evident, and it should be interpreted in conjunction with Blanton's words.

As for Roosevelt himself, he believes that his message is completely clear and does not need further explanation. Therefore, when sending the original text to Congress, he only attached a brief message, pointing out that economic and political stability is now threatened by selfish interests and the danger of conflict, and strongly advocating the necessity of reducing armaments and abandoning weapons of aggression. Most international disputes arise from fear of aggression by others. The message did not ask Congress to pass it, but only said it was for information only. (16th Kuo Min dispatch)

(Washington) The two articles published by President Roosevelt have been hailed by Congress as great and timely remarks, demonstrating the excellent character of world leaders. Speaker Rainey predicts that the American people will enthusiastically and unanimously support the proposal to stand on the same front to restrain aggressor nations. It is hoped that German Chancellor Hitler and his peers can accept the meaning and spirit of the US President's declaration. (16th Reuters dispatch)

American Newspapers Call it a Magna Carta of Humanity 50

French Newspapers Unanimously Disappointed

British Newspapers' Comments Show Differing Views

(London) President Roosevelt's declaration is welcomed by American public opinion, with one Boston newspaper even calling it a Magna Carta of humanity. However, French newspapers unanimously expressed disappointment, as the declaration did not indicate that the United States was prepared to jointly guarantee peace in Europe. The Parisian newspaper Le Journal stated that the US President is again asking us to disarm without an equal guarantee. A far-right French newspaper stated that it would be more beneficial if Hitler could resolutely issue a clear and decisive statement, as moderate words only mislead people. (17th Reuters dispatch)

(London) British newspapers commented on President Roosevelt's declaration today, unanimously praising its spirit, but differing in their views on the value of these remarks in the overall European situation. The London Times stated that this is the most insightful statement advocating concerted action in the political and economic spheres, and is rarely heard from various countries. There is no doubt that it can receive the full support of the British Empire. However, this support may not be so easily obtained from several countries on the European continent. Although the US President has not been able to bind the United States to engage in armed intervention to protect the interests of the invaded, he has repeatedly stated the US's readiness to participate in consultation agreements, which is extremely important. The Hwi-wen-pao (News Summary) commented more realistically, saying that after the United States issued this declaration, it immediately canceled its position of not hearing about foreign affairs and has become somewhat bound. In the future, if there are those who violate the new peace promises, it will directly intervene to show its disapproval. The Dien-wen-pao (Telegraph News) and Chen-yu-pao (Morning Post) both mentioned that the United States did not guarantee peace in Europe and both said that what Europe needs is a guarantee that the United States will express its disapproval through practical intervention in the event of war. Most critics said that Hitler's remarks today could determine the fate of the Disarmament Conference. The first condition for progress in disarmament is that Germany abandons its demand to preserve a long-term conscript army. The future of disarmament depends solely on whether there is an indication in the German Chancellor's remarks that Germany can abandon this demand. The biggest test of Hitler's political skill will be seen in this speech. The Financial Times said that the meeting of German foreign creditors in Berlin is a sign that Germany cannot continue to remit money to repay its debts, but for truly impoverished debtor nations, it is more beneficial to future trade to provide them with some assistance than to force them to pay off their debts. (17th Reuters dispatch)

Page 7

Hitler's Important Speech 51

Firmly Demands Equality in Armaments

Constantly Thinking of Revising the Treaty

(Berlin) German Chancellor Hitler stated in his speech to the Reichstag today that he completely denies any intention of plunging Europe into another war, but there was an intense declaration that Germany is determined to restore its equal status in the international community. He then proclaimed that a European war cannot improve the current situation. Hitler bitterly attacked the Treaty of Versailles and its military and economic provisions, saying that Germany has suicidally fulfilled unreasonable reparations with loyalty. He also said that the Treaty of Versailles completely failed to make political borders coincide with natural borders. The inequality of the treaty was entirely caused by the prevailing mentality among the warring countries at the time, as major countries held preconceived notions, wanting to prove that Germany was the sole instigator of war. Hitler also denounced the League of Nations for losing its original purpose and becoming a tool for armed powers to maintain their authority, saying that the League of Nations has never given genuine assistance to weak countries. International agreements and accords only have genuine value between countries with equal international rights. Hitler warned of the crisis of communism destroying world culture, saying that a new war in Europe would only result in new sacrifices for all warring countries, leading to new insecurity and ultimately creating a situation of communist unrest. Hitler declared that revising the Treaty of Versailles is not only necessary in Germany's view, but other countries themselves have also anticipated that it will need to be revised. Hitler then elaborated on the three main goals of the National Socialist Party from the beginning, saying that the National Socialist revolution first sought to eliminate communism, second to solve Germany's unemployment problem, and third to establish a strong government to become an active collaborator in future agreements with other countries. He also said that Germany completely sympathizes with the same desires of other countries. German youth deeply know the suffering they have experienced and do not want to inflict this suffering on other countries. When discussing the necessity of revising the Treaty of Versailles, Hitler assured that Germany would not use force to break any agreements, even if the agreement clearly needs to be replaced by a better agreement, Germany does not want to use force to achieve it. The past fourteen years have shown that dividing the world into victors and vanquished only increases the suffering of all countries. Regardless of victory or defeat, they all suffer the same. Hitler also said that the Treaty of Versailles acknowledges that Germany can morally demand that other countries disarm. We do not want what we are unwilling to give to others. Hitler denied that the National Socialist Storm Troopers were an army, declaring that anyone who says that Germany has not honorably fulfilled all the disarmament clauses of the Treaty of Versailles is not being fair or accurate. He then welcomed the US President's declaration with the most enthusiastic language, claiming that Germany is ready to join any non-aggression pact, but then made a surprising statement, declaring that if Germany is not granted equality in armaments, Germany will withdraw from the League of Nations, because it is most difficult to force Germany to remain a member of the League of Nations as a second-class country. Germany cannot be forced to sign an agreement that will permanently prevent it from being a first-class country, and neither threats nor intimidation can impress the German people and government. Hitler concluded by declaring that if they want to deprive Germany of its due rights by a majority vote, Germany will be prepared to withdraw from any conference without hesitation. During Hitler's speech, applause frequently thundered from the seats of the deputies, including the former Crown Prince. The speech was unanimously adopted immediately after its conclusion. (17th Kuo Min dispatch)

(London) It is heard that the British representative to the Disarmament Conference, Eden, is scheduled to return to Geneva today to participate in tomorrow's important meeting. Foreign Minister Simon will go to Geneva next week to participate in the League of Nations Council meeting, but he is not expected to attend this week's Disarmament Conference. (17th Reuters dispatch)

British Ambassador to Japan

Openly Defends Japan 52

(London) When the British ambassador to Japan, Sir Francis Lindley, recently passed through Canada, he spoke to guests about Japan's policy regarding Manchuria, expressing considerable sympathy for Japan. When the House of Commons met today, several members questioned this. Foreign Minister Simon replied that he could not criticize this matter until he had met with Lindley. The British government's policy has been clearly established, which is to faithfully abide by the report passed by the League of Nations General Assembly on February 24. As for the news reported by the Ottawa newspaper, he could not say that it was entirely accurate. (17th Reuters dispatch)

Lu Shiting

Planning the Development of Mengshan 58

(Jinan) Lu Shiting, the special commissioner for the investigation and development of Mengshan, has returned to Jinan with the magistrate of Mengyin County to report. Mengshan is surrounded by four to five hundred li and spans the four counties of Yishui, Mengyin, Fei, and Sishui. The area within Mengyin County has been surveyed. The mountain has many natural large forests, fertile soil, and abundant springs. Agricultural products are abundant, with peanuts being the main crop. There are over a hundred kinds of medicinal materials. Foxes and giant snakes are the most numerous. It was occupied by bandits for over ten years. Sixty to seventy villages in the mountains have been burned down. Only one of the seventy to eighty villages below the mountain was not breached by the bandits. The people have fled in all directions, and the fields are barren. Now that the bandits have been cleared, the people are gradually returning. The products of Mengshan within Fei County are especially abundant. There is a peak called Guangding Mountain, where over a hundred people live, who do not interact with the people below the mountain. Lu Shiting has decided to develop Mengshan, first ordering the four counties of Yi, Si, Fei, and Meng to protect the forests in the mountains. (17th special dispatch)

Page 8

Truth Revealed in the Inukai Assassination Case 84

▲United Press Tokyo, 17th -- The Justice Department announced the details of the assassination case of Prime Minister Inukai, which shook Japanese politics, at 5 PM today. The Ministry of Interior also lifted the ban on reporting on it. The content is very long, totaling seventeen pages. The following is an excerpt of the outline:

(Purpose of the Assassination) 85

According to the confessions of the 47 arrested perpetrators, they were indignant at the corruption and degradation of political parties and the extreme tyranny of the Zaibatsu. They believed that such collusion of privileges and factions was unthinkable for the future of the country. In order to eliminate the traitors by the emperor's side and reform national politics, there was no other way but to use extraordinary means to overthrow political parties, Zaibatsu, and privileged classes. The comrades were planning this, and Inoue Akira (alias Shao) and others had already started working in February, assassinating Inoue Junnosuke (former Minister of Finance) and Dan Takuma (representative of Mitsui Zaibatsu). Many of their comrades had been arrested and could not carry out their ambitions. In March, they contacted the Blood Oath Corps Inoue and others to plan the May 15th Incident.

(Process of the Uprising) 86

The work of the May 15th Assassination was divided into two aspects. The military was divided into three groups. The first group was further divided into two subgroups, A and B. Group A of the first group, led by Navy Lieutenant Commander Mikami Taku, along with Navy Reserve Ensign Kuroiwa, Yagi, Ishizeki, and Goto Eihan, gathered at Yasukuni Shrine, put on military uniforms, and traveled by car, going to the Prime Minister's official residence and the Metropolitan Police Department. At 5:40 PM, Lieutenant Commander Mikami personally opened fire and killed Prime Minister Inukai, and patrolmen Tanaka and Hirayama. Patrolman Tanaka died on the spot. Ensign Kuroiwa commanded officers and students to bomb the Metropolitan Police Department. Group B of the first group, led by Navy Lieutenant Commander Yamagishi, along with Navy Ensign Murayama, Shinohara, and Army Officer Cadets Nomura, assisted Group A in bombing the Prime Minister's official residence and the Metropolitan Police Department. The special duty of this group was to bomb the Bank of Japan. The second group was led by Navy Lieutenant Commander Koga, along with students from the Army Officer School Camp, Sakamoto, Nishikawa, and Ikematsu, who gathered in front of the graves of the Forty-Seven Ronin (loyal and righteous retainers of the Tokugawa era) at Sengakuji Temple. They split into groups to bomb the Metropolitan Police Department and Minister of the Imperial Household Makino. Koga threw a hand grenade at the gate of Minister Makino's residence and shot and wounded Patrolman Hashii. On the way from the Makino residence to the Metropolitan Police Department, they scattered leaflets along the way and threw a grenade at the Metropolitan Police Department, injuring Secretary Nagasaka and Takahashi, a reporter for the Yomiuri Shimbun. The third group was led by Navy Lieutenant Commander Nakamura, along with officer students Nakajima, Kaneshiro, and Min Yoshihara, who gathered at Shinbashi Station. They first bombed the Seiyukai headquarters, then drove to the Metropolitan Police Department. The three groups' actions all aimed at bombing the Metropolitan Police Department as their final destination. After achieving their goals, they went to the Tokyo Military Police headquarters to surrender, stating the details of their crimes. Twenty members of the Peasant Suicide Squad were all commanded by Tachibana Kosaburo, head of the Aikyo Juku, and Honma Kenichiro, head of the Shizan Juku, and were responsible for bombing the power plant and Mitsubishi Bank, and assassinating the rebel comrade Lieutenant Nishida. Their respective tasks were as follows: (1) The Tokyo Electric Yodobashi Power Plant was the responsibility of Onzui Hidenori, who threw a grenade at the cold water pipe at 7:40 PM. (2) The Tabata Power Plant was the responsibility of Hanawa Iohae, who threw a grenade at 7:10 PM, but it did not detonate. (3) The Kameido Power Plant was the responsibility of Yabuki Masami, who threw a grenade at 8:00 PM, but it did not detonate. He destroyed its transfer machine. (4) The Mejiro Power Plant was the responsibility of Komuro Rikiya, who threw a grenade at 7:00 PM, but was arrested. (5) The Hatogaya Power Plant was the responsibility of Yokosuka Kikuo, who threw a grenade at 7:00 PM and destroyed part of it. (6) The Kinu Electric Tokyo Power Plant was the responsibility of Onuki Akiharu and Takanezawa Ichi, who threw a hand grenade and destroyed its water bottle and transfer machine. (7) Mitsubishi Bank was the responsibility of Meiji University student Okuda Hideo, who threw two grenades at 7:00 PM and destroyed its glass windows. (8) The assassination of the rebel comrade Lieutenant Nishida was the responsibility of Kawasaki Nagamitsu, who shot Nishida, wounding him but not killing him.

(The Mastermind Behind the Case) 87

The masterminds behind this case were Dr. Okawa Shumei, chairman of the Jinmu Society, Toyama Hidesan, chairman of the Tenko Society, Inoue Akira, head of the Blood Oath Corps, Tachibana Kosaburo, head of the Aikyo Juku, and Honma Kenichiro, head of the Shizan Juku.

Okawa's brief history: Okawa Shumei is 49 years old, from Yamagata Prefecture, and graduated from the Fifth Higher School, the same class as former Ambassador to China Shigemitsu Aoi. Later, he entered the Faculty of Arts of Tokyo Imperial University, studied philosophy, and later changed his mindset and turned to research on national reconstruction. He obtained a doctorate in the Taisho 15th year. When he was a translator for the Army General Staff Headquarters, he had a close relationship with General Watanabe. In the Taisho 7th year, he became a professor at Takushoku University, in the 8th year he was the director of the East Asia Economic Survey Bureau, in the 14th year he was appointed as a director of South Manchuria Railway, and in the Showa 4th year he was the director of the East Asia Economic Survey Bureau. Among his friends are Toyama Mitsuru, Uchida Ryohei, and Indian independence party member Haas. (Japan United Press)

Source of Weapons 88

The source of weapons and military funds is as follows: (1) The weapons consisted of 13 pistols, 13 hand grenades, and 7 Japanese swords. Among them, Okawa supplied 5 pistols, Honma supplied 6, the military provided 1, and others were supplied by Major Fujii and the Kwantung Army. (2) Military funds: Okawa Shumei disbursed 5,000 yuan in three installments. (3) 7,600 yuan was robbed by Akanuma.

(Arrest of the Perpetrators) 89

Starting with the Blood Oath Corps assassinations, this bloody incident occurred on May 15th. The military perpetrators included 11 students from the Army Officer School and 16 naval officers, totaling 27. They surrendered that night. Most of the Peasant Suicide Squad were also arrested. However, Tachibana Kosaburo, head of the Aikyo Juku, and Haruta Nobuyoshi fled to Manchuria and were arrested on July 24th. Honma Kenichiro, head of the Shizan Juku, was arrested in Tokyo on September 18th. Okawa Shumei was arrested in a car on June 15th. Toyama Hidesan, head of the Tenko Society, and Dr. Maki and others were arrested on November 5th after intimidation. Yamada Chuichi, a student of the Aikyo Juku, was arrested twice for attempting to appeal directly to the Emperor for the pardon of his comrades, a total of five people. There were a total of 47 perpetrators directly related to the May 15th Incident. The list of their names is omitted.

▲Japan United Press -- All military criminals in this case surrendered themselves. However, civilian criminals fled separately after the incident. The following is a brief description of the investigation of its main characters.

Dr. Okawa Shumei, Doctor of Law: Okawa Shumei boarded a train from Tokyo Ueno Station to Aomori City on June 15, Showa 7, to attend a Shinbukan lecture. The Metropolitan Police Department suspected that he was involved in the May 15th incident, because he guided the young officers of the Army and Navy, and used explosives with the □□ Action Team. They dispatched five plainclothes officers to arrest Okawa on the train and got off at Ueno Station. He was then taken to the Metropolitan Police Department, and after the Prosecutor's Office investigated, he was detained in Ichigaya Prison, and was accused of violating the Explosives Control Act and of inciting murder.

Tachibana Kosaburo: Tachibana secretly went to Manchuria with his secretary, Haruta Nobuyoshi, after the incident. Haruta was arrested in Changchun and fled to Harbin, hiding in a Russian house. The Metropolitan Police Department sent seven police officers to Manchuria, but failed to capture Tachibana and only captured Haruta and returned him to Japan. Tachibana planned to rebuild the party headquarters in Harbin, but after his comrades were arrested one after another, Tachibana also felt the danger around him, and surrendered to the Harbin Military Police on July 24. Tachibana was the principal of Aikyo Juku. He established Aikyo Juku in his hometown of Mito. Because of his noble personality, the number of peasant children increased day by day. In Showa 5, he expanded the organization and named it "Self-Art Rural Labor School Aikyo Juku". The spirit he guides is to integrate the three principles of land, brotherhood, and labor. Its main purpose is to cultivate practical fighters who realize agrarian Japanese nationalism.

Toyama Hidesan, Chairman of the Tenko Society: Toyama Hidesan, the third son of the famous Toyama Mitsuru. As the Metropolitan Police Department did not know his whereabouts, after serious investigation, they learned that he was hiding in Suginami District, Tokyo. On November 5, they organized an armed team to surround his house and arrest Uratoyama and several of his men. At the same time, police officers were sent to the Tenko Society headquarters, Toyama Mitsuru's house, the National Ideology Research Association, and the East Asia Economic Bureau to discover pistols, Japanese swords, and other evidence.

(Punishment of the Defendants) 90

▲Dentsu News Agency Tokyo, 17th -- Okawa Shumei and others, who were defendants as civilians in the May 15th Incident, could not be prosecuted for the crime of mutiny by the Army and Navy, so they were prosecuted for murder, attempted murder, and violation of the Explosives Control Act. Navy Captain Hama Yuji was ill, so he was dealt with separately. The other Army and Navy defendants were expected to be prosecuted for mutiny as planned.

(Japanese Cabinet Trembles) 91

▲Japan United Press Tokyo, 17th -- After the government announced the May 15th Incident, the political situation will change, which is a common observation among people. Therefore, the issue of Finance Minister Takahashi's advance or retreat is now attracting attention from all sides. Prime Minister Saito is considering various measures to extend the life of the cabinet and wants to retain the Finance Minister. The Prime Minister plans to observe the political situation for a few days after the announcement of the May 15th Incident, and will meet with the Finance Minister next week to persuade him to abandon his intention to resign.

(Saito Maintains Silence) 92

▲Dentsu News Agency Tokyo, 17th -- The content of the May 15th Incident has been announced today. Prime Minister Saito did not express any feelings, because he feared a major social reaction. As for the Army's view on the announcement of the May 15th Incident, as some have argued, because the emergency has not yet been resolved, it cannot be a reason for the current cabinet to resign en masse.

(Ogaki's Recollection) 93

▲Dentsu News Agency Tokyo, 17th -- After the May 15th Incident was announced, Navy Minister Ogaki recalled his feelings as follows: "Young officers were angry at the phenomena of the country and society, and such an incident occurred, which is very pitiful. Because of public anger and righteous indignation, they violated national law, and their direct actions cannot be tolerated. Moreover, it is fearful for active-duty soldiers to act according to their own will. It is only natural for us military personnel to uphold the Emperor's will and purify military discipline. Furthermore, the Japanese people should reflect on themselves, avoid making further mistakes, and strive for the best."

Japan's Ming Lun Hui Established 94

Advocating Maintaining the Imperial Way and Reforming the Political World

▲Dentsu 17th Tokyo -- With General Tanaka Kuniaki at the center, the Ming Lun Hui, which aims to maintain the restoration of the Imperial Way and reform the political world, brought together 30,000 retired civil and military officials. Yesterday afternoon, after praying in front of the Imperial Palace, a grand inaugural ceremony was held at the Tokyo Kaikan.

Japanese Troops Press on All Sides, Approaching Beiping and Tianjin, Situation is Serious 95

--- Convey

Enemy Crossing the Luan River, News East of Tangshan is Chaotic

Shixia Falls, Enemy Attacks Miyun, Our Troops Fight Hard

Beiping's City Defense is Tight, Sandbags Piled in Streets and Alleys

Beiping Special Dispatch: The Japanese army is harboring an extremely large conspiracy to invade and harass Beiping and Tianjin. The first step of their plan is to occupy Luanzhou in the east and capture Miyun in the west, so that the barriers of Beiping and Tianjin are completely removed and there is no danger to defend. The second step is to copy the rear roads of Beiping and Tianjin, cut off the connection between Beiping and Tianjin along the Pingyu Highway in the east, and attack the key towns of the Pinghan Road in the west to surround Beiping. When the second step of the plan is completed, the traitors who have been bought in advance will simultaneously carry out large-scale riots in Beiping and Tianjin, causing internal changes in Beiping and Tianjin, so as to achieve their conspiracy and reap the benefits. The first step of their plan has been completed, and the second step is underway. As for the purchase of traitors, although it has been greatly hit due to Zhang Jingyao's assassination, those of his kind who have not yet been captured are still extremely active. The Japanese army's purpose is to focus on the three northeastern provinces and Rehe and Chahar. If they can truly occupy the above provinces and complete their so-called Manchu-Mongolian policy, they can temporarily stop. Their various conspiracies against Guannei are nothing but attempts to achieve this goal. Therefore, if Beiping and Tianjin are lost, their approach will be different from the tricks they played in the three northeastern provinces. Our authorities regard Beiping and Tianjin as the lifeline of the north. If Beiping and Tianjin have any problems, not only the north will be shaken, but the whole country will also be shaken. They vowed to defend them with all their strength and contend with the powerful enemy. Now is a critical moment. Let's see how the situation develops in the next few days.

The Japanese and puppet troops who invaded again, that is, those who forced their way across the river on the 12th in separate routes, advanced towards Renzikou, Gaotaizi from Dongxizhai, and pressed towards Shaheyi after crossing the river from Lulong. The puppet army Li Jichun's troops were responsible for gradually pressing westward on the front of the railway. In the past two days, the enemy at Shaheyi has forced Leizhuang, Guye, and Gaotaizi to the west of Luanzhou in the south, and the enemy at Renzikou has attacked Fengrun. Because the rear road of Luanzhou area was threatened and feared to be heavily surrounded, our army has concentrated a large army in the Tangshan area since yesterday. He Zhuguo and Wan Fulin also moved to a certain place west of Tangshan to direct military affairs. The enemy army adopted an offensive method, and did not fight along the railway line. They are purely dividing their forces north of the railway to advance, and our army is also defending everywhere north of the railway line to prevent the enemy army from penetrating deeply, and fighting hard with the enemy. This morning (15th), the enemy army attacked Fengrun in a big way. Fengrun City has been bombed by enemy planes for several days, which is very tragic. There are about one division of our army in that area, and they are currently fighting fiercely. The enemy army is paying special attention to Fengrun, and is conspiring to occupy Fengrun, attack Song's troops in the north, and establish contact with the Japanese army at Xifengkou. To attack Yutian in the west, and force Tangshan in the south, threatening the rear of our army, so they must obtain Fengrun.

After the Japanese army in the Gubeikou area launched a full-line general attack, our army fought bravely and fought fiercely for three days and nights. Both sides suffered heavy casualties. Our army's position was completely destroyed due to the pressure of the enemy's airplanes, artillery, and tanks. Since yesterday, our army has withdrawn to the new position pre-constructed south of Shixia. Yesterday, the fierce battle lasted all day, and the enemy did not succeed. Today, the enemy's casualties were too heavy, and they were waiting for replenishment, and they did not launch a large-scale attack. The war was slightly gentler than in the past two days. Now, our army's front line is in the Jiusongling area, 30 miles north of Miyun, only more than 150 miles away from Beiping. In order to prevent the enemy army from advancing south, our army has transferred a large army to reinforce it, and has deployed defenses section by section south of Jiusongling, and the position is quite solid. From 5:00 AM this morning (15th), Japanese planes flew back and forth to Miyun five times to drop bombs, and used machine guns to strafe, causing losses to residents.

In order to intimidate our rear, the Japanese army sent planes to reconnaissance and drop bombs in various places every day. In addition to sending leaflets to Ping twice, they also sent five planes to Baoding for reconnaissance yesterday afternoon. This morning, three Japanese planes also dropped bombs in the Tangshan area, causing slight damage to the ground.

In Beiping, the situation has become increasingly serious in recent days. In order to prevent villains from taking the opportunity to harass, the authorities have piled sandbags in important streets and alleys since yesterday morning, and curfew has been imposed earlier at night. Last night, more than 400 suspicious traitors were found in small hotels and remote places. Secret symbols were found in their collars and under their arms, and they have been detained for strict investigation. The Japanese army originally planned to hold an exercise this morning, but seeing that our side was heavily guarded and fearing accidents, they temporarily stopped. Now, a large army has been stationed in the four suburbs of Beiping, and the defense is solid. All important places inside and outside Beiping city are also equipped with fortifications. If the enemy army invades, they will swear to fight to the death. Even if they turn the cultural area of thousands of years into ruins, they will not hesitate. In Tianjin, the authorities are also paying great attention to security and are strictly guarding against villains causing trouble. (15th)

Hankou Correspondence: Since Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek instructed Liu Zhenhua, Commander-in-Chief of the Henan, Hubei and Anhui Border Area Bandit Suppression, to supervise bandit suppression in eastern Hubei, Liu came to Hankou and convened a bandit suppression meeting with Director He Chengjun to decide on strategies. To flee to the Shaanxi border, it is difficult to achieve its goal due to road repairs and obstructions. Therefore, developing to the east may be its most recent goal. Its two attempts to send bandits to invade Honghu are sufficient proof. Now Xu has arrived in Shashi, and will supervise the division's advance to suppress them, and will also be responsible for clearing the scattered bandits in the border area. Xu has long been in command of the army and is known as a famous general. He's bandits have been repeatedly defeated and fear him like a tiger. Kong's bandits in southern Hubei have recently been defeated by the Hunan army. They once attempted to enter Hubei in two routes. The National Army stationed in Tongshan was Xie Bin's New 10th Division, and the National Army stationed in Yangxin was Guo Rudong's 26th Division, who tried their best to resist the battle, and the bandits were unsuccessful. Southwest Inspection of Mail 97

Dispatching Inspectors to be Permanently Stationed at the Bureau for Office Work

Guangdong Postal Workers Union Forms Investigation Team to Assist

Guangzhou Correspondence, Propaganda Group of the Southwest Executive Department: Considering the severity of the national crisis recently, and the difficulty in ensuring that important cities in the Southwest are free of spies, in order to strictly prevent such occurrences, in addition to separately establishing methods for handling telegram inspections, with regards to the inspection of mail, a special request has been submitted to the Southwest Executive Department, instructing the Southwest Political Affairs Committee to instruct the provincial governments of the Southwest to order the public security bureaus and county governments to dispatch officials to be permanently stationed at post offices to strictly inspect all incoming and outgoing mail in their respective localities, according to the following measures: (1) Mail concerning military, diplomatic, or national defense secrets should be immediately detained; (2) Mail concerning secret communication with communist bandits should be immediately detained; (3) Mail with reactionary wording or suspicious signs should be immediately detained; (4) Mail detained by inspectors should be confidentially submitted to the local government for investigation; (5) The local government should immediately investigate such mail, and report important cases to higher authorities. The Guangdong Provincial Government received this order yesterday, ordering the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau to dispatch personnel to the post office for inspection within a specified time limit. Furthermore, in order to assist party and government agencies in inspecting mail, the local postal workers' union has recently organized a special postal workers' mail investigation team, consisting of one team leader and four small team members. Membership is open to all union members until the quota is filled. The team leader is responsible for the team's affairs under the orders of the postal workers' union. The small team leaders are responsible for managing team members and supervising their respective small teams in carrying out inspections and investigating reactionary propaganda mail and the smuggling of inferior goods using postal packages. If party and government agencies have matters to entrust to the postal workers' union, the union will instruct the team leader to execute them. If any team member discovers suspicious mail or violations of the aforementioned items, they must report them level by level to higher authorities for review. (10th day)

Wuxi 103

Urgent Appeal to Abolish Diesel Tax

Since the oil refining industry was first invented in Guangdong Province, factories have been established in various places, with this city being the most developed. At its peak, there were more than 50 refineries. Recently, due to the dumping of Russian oil and the repeated price drops of kerosene from companies like Meiya, the oil refining market has plummeted. Refiners have been unable to maintain operations, and two-thirds have closed down. Furthermore, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance has dispatched a special commissioner to establish a bureau in this city to collect oil refining business tax, which refiners already find difficult to bear. Unexpectedly, the customs authorities have also proposed levying an import tax on diesel oil of 2.90 gold units per ton. If used for refining kerosene, an additional 23.40 gold units will be levied. Oil refineries believe that the current cost of raw materials is already expensive and unprofitable. If this new tax is implemented, the oil refining industry will be destroyed. Jiangsu province's oil refiners Yongji Xu Shutang, Dahua Wei Haoran, Meili Zhou Yongnian, Limin Ding Jiefu, Zhonghua Qiang Fengqi, etc., in order to safeguard the livelihoods of the poor and reclaim rights and interests, jointly submitted a petition to the Jiangsu Provincial Self-Refined Kerosene Business Tax Bureau yesterday, requesting that it be forwarded to the Department of Finance and various ministries and courts, citing the Guangdong precedent, to immediately abolish the new diesel tax, so that the dying refiners of Jiangsu province may have a chance to recover.

Truth Revealed in the Swallowing Stolen Pigs Case 104

Yang Zuxun, the head of the fourth Jia of the Fifth District Sitou Town Security Corps, and others, the case of swallowing the stolen pigs, the situation has been briefly described in this newspaper. It is now known that on the twelfth day of last month at midnight, the pig boat of boatmen Liu Afa and Wang Laowu was robbed at Shangshun Bridge, Zhangjing, Fifth District of this city. Yang Zuxun, the head of the Jia, happened to be leading the corps members near the No. 3 Bridge on Xicheng Road and intercepted two stolen boats and thirty-eight large pigs. Wang Mingshan, the class leader of the Jia, and Zhang Panquan, the corps member, discussed selling the large pigs the next morning to Tan Yaobing's butcher shop in Sitou Town for nine pigs, Shen Bohua's butcher shop for nine pigs, and Lu Julin's butcher shop for three pigs, for a total of 479.5 yuan. The remaining fifteen pigs were sent to the district corps headquarters. The owner, Wang Laowu, paid 105 yuan to redeem thirteen pigs. After April 20th, County Magistrate Yan learned of the matter from a newspaper report and secretly ordered Wu Deqing, the director of the Public Security Bureau, and Song Zhentao, the director of the Security Corps, to investigate. Director Song immediately sent instructor Zhang Qisen to the countryside for a secret investigation, which revealed that the incident did occur. County Magistrate Yan then summoned Jiang Jiayou, the district corps leader, corps member Li Guohua, Zhang Panquan, Zhu Shengyang, instructor Ge Zhen, and butcher shop owners Tan Yaobing, Lu Julin, You Zixun, and butcher Zou Ahe to the case one after another. Yao Fusun, a staff member of the secretariat, opened a court and repeatedly interrogated them. Each person knew that it was difficult to conceal the truth and revealed the truth. At the same time, boatman Liu Afa also surrendered and stated the process. Until the previous (15th) day, Yang Zuxun, the head of the fourth Jia, also knew that the matter had been exposed and surrendered himself to the county, directly admitting to selling the pigs, only claiming that he intended to buy firearms with the money. He also claimed that after the county committee sent a secret investigation to the countryside, he entrusted instructor Ge Zhen to come to the city for activities. According to instructor Ge, he once contacted Zhang Qisen, a secret investigator of the county Security Corps, and Zhang demanded an activity fee of 800 yuan. Because the amount was too large, it was not successful. Later, Hu Bin (Zhen Qian), the current section chief of the Second Section of the Public Security Bureau, learned of the matter and invited Yu to meet at the Donghu Hotel. Hu said that he could find a way, and Yu had a close relationship with Yang and could not refuse, so he temporarily accepted it and stored it in the Donghu Hotel, intending to return the original items after the case was over. The 150 yuan in silver was not received. After the confession, Hu immediately called the Donghu Hotel and ordered the tea room to send the goldware to the county for presentation. Finally, Yao questioned Yang Zuxun again, and it was not until 11:00 p.m. that it was over. As a result, the court ordered Hu Bin, Yang Zuxun, and Ge Zhen to be taken care of together. At the same time, the director of the Security Corps, Song Zhentao, was ordered to transfer Zhang Qisen to the case for interrogation and detention yesterday, and County Magistrate Yan ordered Hu Bin to be dismissed. The vacant position was concurrently filled by Ji Nianru, the section chief of the First Section of the Public Security Bureau. Yesterday (16th) afternoon, County Magistrate Yan prepared a document and transferred Hu Bin, Yang Zuxun, Zhang Qisen, Lu Julin, Ge Zhen, Zhang Panquan, Li Guohua, Zhu Shengyang and other eight people to the County Court, where Prosecutor Shen interrogated them closely. The court ordered them to be detained together and await verification.

Fish Tax Increase Leads to Fish Market Strike

Pinghu 108

Japanese Warship Sails into Zhapu

On the 15th, near dusk, two warships were discovered on the sea off Zhapu, speeding from outside Caiqi Gate. The hulls were all black and gradually entered the restricted area. Finally, they docked outside the Tianfei Palace on the sea embankment. The people of Zhapu thought they were domestic cruisers, but upon closer inspection, they saw that the flags of Japan were hanging at the stern of the ships. One ship also clearly stated "Dai Nippon No. 27 Destroyer". Each ship was equipped with four large cannons and eight or nine small cannons. There were many soldiers in the cabins. The people of Zhapu were greatly alarmed upon seeing this and rushed to inform the local security team soldiers. At that time, the ships lowered sampans and openly landed soldiers, totaling four soldiers and one sailor, but all were in plainclothes. The team soldiers stepped forward and politely advised them to return to the ship, but these people glared fiercely and were unreasonable. One of them, speaking Chinese, said they wanted to seek medical treatment and buy fruit. The team soldiers had no choice but to accompany them to the main street, where they bought a small amount of oranges and other items, but did not seek medical treatment. They strolled around for a long time before reluctantly returning to the ship, weighing anchor and leaving. Some said that they also saw a giant ship anchored in the outer sea that had not sailed in. That night, all districts of this county, upon hearing the news, intensified their vigilance.

Xiaoshan 109

Four People Drown While Testing Water Volume

The seawall along the Qiantang River has been in disrepair for many years, and the stone embankments along the dike are often eroded by the tides. In order to protect the embankment, the Water Conservancy Bureau specially set up a sluice gate, the Xixing Temporary Engineering Office, and the Water Conservancy Bureau for Repairing and Maintaining Rivers. In order to prevent contractors from cutting corners, Su Huanxiang, an official, was specially dispatched to supervise the section. On the afternoon of the 13th, at about 1:00 p.m., Su, along with Shao Lieqiao, the son of contractor Shao, and seven sailors, were on a sampan testing the depth of the water when the tide suddenly surged, capsizing the sampan. Four of the seven drowned. The bodies of Shao Lieqiao, Su Huanxiang, and two workers drifted to the river mouth and have not been found. It was not until about 5:00 p.m. that the bodies were recovered on the Xixing Riverbank.

Local News

Second Municipal Federation National Goods Movement Propaganda Meeting 111

Held yesterday at the Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association

Ji Zejin Speaks on the National Goods Crisis

Entire Body Swears to Use National Goods

The First Special District Citizens Federation, in order to promote national goods, held the Second National Goods Movement Propaganda Meeting at the Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association yesterday at 1 p.m. Details are recorded below:

Representatives Present 112

Those who attended yesterday included Ji Zejin, Director and Secretary of the International Trade Guidance Department of the Ministry of Industry; Lin Kanghou of the Banking Association; Hu Fengxiang, Wang Hanliang, Wu Zhihao, Zhang Yichen, Chen Jicheng, Yu Zhongxian, Tao Leqin, Wang Honghui, Zheng Dongshan, Cao Zhigong, Chen Jiufeng, Chen Binghui, Fang Peicheng, Zhu Yangwu, Zhang Xianfang of various district branches of the Citizens Federation; and guests from all walks of life, totaling more than 750 people. Lin Kanghou, Wang Hanliang, Wu Zhihao, Hu Fengxiang, Zhang Yichen, Chen Jicheng, Yu Zhongxian, Chen Binghui, Liu Zhongying, and other nine people formed the presidium.

Chairman's Report 113

After the meeting began with customary formalities, Chairman Wang Hanliang first gave a speech, stating that the association, in order to promote national goods and resist foreign goods, held the First National Goods Movement Propaganda Meeting on April 9. However, because practical work has not shown much effectiveness, a second propaganda meeting is being held today. The purpose is to enable national goods to be sold well at home and abroad, and to solve the current domestic business difficulties. It is hoped that all those present will do their best to publicize, and at the same time, fundamentally realize the true meaning of today's meeting.

Ji Zejin's Speech 114

Next, Ji Zejin, Secretary of the International Trade Bureau, gave a speech, stating that in recent years, the sales of national goods in our country have been sluggish, and imported goods have flooded the market, resulting in a leakage of hundreds of millions of dollars every year. The reasons for this are nothing more than the dumping of foreign goods in China, the binding of our country's tariffs by treaties, and the lack of organization of domestic enterprises. Therefore, national goods are difficult to compete with foreign goods. If this continues, the future of national goods in our country is very dangerous. The International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, in order to save

Second Municipal Federation National Goods Movement Propaganda Meeting (Photo by Xu Tianzhang) 115

China's industry and promote the sales of national goods, has specifically formulated opinions for the reference of national goods manufacturers: (1) "Dumping of Foreign Goods". After the European War, various countries worked hard to produce. Internally, they reduced export taxes and encouraged exports, and externally, they increased import taxes to make it difficult for foreign goods to enter and compete with their domestic industries. As a result, production became increasingly developed, with supply exceeding demand. The domestic market could not accommodate these surplus goods, so in order to save their economic panic, they had to seek markets abroad to accommodate their surplus products. China's industry is backward and its population is large, making it the only large market for foreign powers to sell goods. Therefore, various countries compete for the exclusive right to this market, dumping their goods on each other. Our country's nascent industry is naturally difficult to compete with cheap and high-quality foreign goods. Therefore, our national goods are greatly impacted. In order to save the national goods industry, the Ministry of Industry has sent special personnel to investigate the situation of foreign goods dumping in China, and then levy anti-dumping duties to restrict them, and use various methods to prevent foreign goods from dumping in China. (2) "China has no tariff protection". Before the outbreak of the European War, after the United Kingdom adopted free trade, because of the fierce competition for dumping in foreign markets, the United Kingdom changed its policy, abandoned the free dumping plan, and implemented protective tariffs. It made every effort to promote emerging industries and imposed extremely high taxes on newly imported industrial products from foreign countries to restrict their import. In China, due to the constraints of various treaties, it cannot compete with other countries, and China's industrial level is still in its infancy. Under this pressure, it is even more difficult to develop. The remedies are divided into (A) increasing import taxes and (B) After the 15th of this month, the Sino-Japanese tariffs have been abolished, and imported goods will be subject to surcharges, which is also a good opportunity to promote national goods. (3) "Chinese National Goods Commit Suicide Due to Competition". Domestic national goods manufacturers reduce prices and sell cheaply due to competition from the same industry. Because of price reductions and cheap sales, the manufacturers' profits are reduced, and various malpractices occur: (A) Factories go bankrupt due to losses, (B) Aspiring industrialists who follow are hesitant to move forward, (C) Price reductions and cheap sales require reducing costs, so each manufacturer cuts corners, resulting in the goods produced losing the trust of users, giving foreign goods an opportunity to intervene. The remedies are divided into (A) National goods factories should unite and supervise each other, so that the prices of all products have certain standards for raw materials and manufacturing, and (B) The Ministry of Industry should have measures to reward industry. (4) "Difficulty in Distinguishing Between National Goods and Foreign Goods" (Fault Lies with National Goods Factories) National goods manufacturers, in order to take advantage of the psychology of the general public with shallow knowledge who prefer to buy foreign goods, use markings similar to those of foreign goods in various products, or do not add Chinese characters on them. As a result, the general knowledgeable class or those who love national goods feel difficult to distinguish. The remedies are divided into (A) should be banned, (B) All national goods should promote the characteristics of China to make it easier for Chinese people to recognize them. (5) "Foreign Goods Impersonate National Goods". Most of the foreign goods imported into China do not have the manufacturer's name and markings, or even change their appearance and blend in, adding the words "Made in China" and adding Chinese trademarks, making it difficult for Chinese people to distinguish between genuine and fake, which in turn makes the national goods market stagnant. This is also a major reason why national goods cannot be dumped. The remedies are divided into (A) Starting in 1934, all foreign goods imported into China will be marked with the country and place of manufacture, (B) Or give inspection, inspection of the consular certificate regarding the source of the goods, if it can be implemented accordingly, national goods can be revitalized.

Speech Also Recorded 116

Next, Wu Zhihao gave a speech, saying that everyone who comes here should know that Chinese people should buy Chinese goods. The reason why North China fell into the hands of the Japanese is that foreign goods were dumped, giving the Japanese economic control. At the same time, they used the money they took from exchanging goods to make guns to fight us. Let us think about how they treat us. The Chinese people should maintain their existing happiness and do their best to use national goods. Chen Binghui, Wang Honghui, Cao Zhigong, and others then gave speeches. The wording is omitted.

Entire Body Swears Oath 117

The original text of the oath is: "We swear from today to make a great determination to promote national goods, use national goods, and not buy or sell enemy goods or foreign goods. If we break our oath, we are willing to be subjected to the most severe punishment. We solemnly swear."

Performing Arts 118

After each person finished speaking, Yi Fangshuo and Zhang Yier of the performing arts circle performed the famous play "National Goods Save the Country", Pei Yanghua, Lu Qiqi, Jiang Xiaoxiao, Liu Chunshan, and others performed comic dramas, Mo Wuqi performed amazing magic, the Postal Workers Union performed silk and bamboo music and harmonica, and the Minshe Drama Troupe performed dramas. The performances were given free of charge and ended at 8:00 p.m.

Radio Broadcast 119

In order to make the true meaning of promoting national goods clear to the entire city, the association specially invited Yu Zhongxian to give a speech on "National Goods Save the Country" at the Great China Radio Station at 1:00 p.m. yesterday. The original text is: "It is the natural and just responsibility of the people of a country to use their own country's goods. In the world, no country needs a few people to persuade the majority to use its domestic products. Therefore, our movement to promote national goods and encourage the use of national goods is simply a very abnormal thing. However, there are two major parts of the reason for creating abnormality. First, the country is too weak and the doors are open. Foreign goods, no matter what they are, can be imported for dumping. The government is facing financial difficulties and wants to earn more money from tariff revenue, regardless of whether the imported goods conflict with domestic products. It only knows that foreigners' imported goods are willing to pay taxes in accordance with the regulations, so it allows them to enter and compete with our existing domestic goods. As a result, foreign goods flood the market and use dumping methods to reduce prices and fight with us desperately. It is a pity that the domestic industry's fragile foundation cannot withstand the destruction. Therefore, the weak industrial products can only be destroyed. Foreign goods can run rampant in the market. On this point, we can only hope that the government will restrict the import of foreign goods. For industrial products that are already produced domestically, at least to a certain extent, when importing foreign goods of the same type as those already produced domestically, the tariffs should be levied extra heavily, so that after they are imported, they can no longer be discounted for dumping. This is the way to incubate and protect domestic industrial products." The Section

No Statement of Suspension of Business in Banking and Finance Sectors in Peiping and Tientsin 120

Recently, there have been rumors that due to the increasingly tense situation in North China, the banking and finance sectors in Peiping and Tientsin will suspend operations. Yesterday, a reporter inquired about this matter with a person in charge of a bank in this city. According to him, the tense situation in Peiping and Tientsin has indeed affected the local financial sector to a considerable extent. However, the rumor of a complete suspension of business is an overstatement. The financial center of the country is in Shanghai, not Peiping and Tientsin, and the banking and finance businesses in Peiping and Tientsin are branches of Shanghai institutions. The Shanghai institutions have no such intention. The rumor is evidently untrue when verified with the opinions of the banking and finance sectors in Shanghai.

Second, the education of the past few decades should also bear significant blame. This is because the education in recent decades has excessively emphasized superficiality and neglected practicality. Educational policies have focused on outward appearances rather than inner development. The fundamentals of self-reliance, such as diligence and thrift, are not mentioned; instead, extravagance is promoted. The younger generation disdains domestic goods as being unsophisticated and considers foreign goods to be fashionable. Especially intellectuals and wealthy individuals with numerous concubines disregard domestic products entirely. Those with knowledge and wealth are considered the upper class. If those in positions of influence are unwilling to promote domestic products, their sales will undoubtedly suffer. Therefore, those responsible for education should take practical responsibility to subtly influence and train young people in diligence and thrift. Diligence eliminates extravagant thoughts, and thrift makes one not particular about whether something is unsophisticated or not. Our country is founded on agriculture, but even the basic necessity of food is now dependent on foreign goods. The import of rice and wheat is substantial every year, and the domestic prices of rice and wheat are controlled by whether or not foreign rice and wheat are imported. This is extremely dangerous. If a maritime blockade were to occur, wouldn't the country descend into panic due to food shortages? The clothes and other goods used in society, a large portion of which are foreign. In recent years, even the food we eat contains foreign ingredients. However, to rectify this problem, local officials must take responsibility and implement virtuous policies to encourage the people to engage in agriculture, eliminating the cultivation of all non-agricultural products. At the same time, no land should be left uncultivated. In rice and wheat-producing regions, transportation should be developed, so that rice and wheat production is sufficient, and we do not need to rely on foreign goods. Only then can the people's food supply be stabilized. We must use domestic goods to live and work in peace. The current unrest in society and the prevalence of bandits and kidnappers are due to the decline in production and the large number of unemployed people. These unemployed individuals have only two paths: to sit and starve to death or to take risks. The pervasive sense of crisis in society is caused by a portion of the unemployed taking the second path. To alleviate the terror surrounding us, we must strive to use domestic goods, revitalize domestic industries, provide jobs for the unemployed, and ensure that everyone has work, which will lead to social stability. In the past, people often spoke of "domestic troubles and foreign invasions," but the extent of the foreign invasion was merely speculation. Now, the reality of foreign invasion is clearly exposed. Our neighboring country, Japan, with its unlimited aggressive ambitions and wolf-like troops, has invaded our heartland. The four northeastern provinces have been completely lost, and Peiping and Tientsin are also in imminent danger. Half of our great country has been taken. In this critical moment of survival, the entire nation must unite and invigorate, improving industry, agriculture, military preparedness, and politics, and putting everything on the right track. Even if we are currently experiencing national humiliation and territorial loss, we can recover our lost territories and wash away our national shame in five or ten years. We, the people, must unite and work together to find a way out. This means loving and using domestic goods, because loving domestic goods means loving the country, and using domestic goods means supporting domestic industries. No matter how cheap foreign goods are, we will not buy them. No matter how beautiful foreign goods are, we will not use them. If money does not flow out of the country, the nation's vitality will not be depleted, and everything can be strengthened. At the same time, we must resolve to boycott Japanese goods. This will eliminate Japan's current display of power, rendering all its warships and cannons ineffective. Japan's finances rely on us. If we impose a long-term economic blockade on Japan, it will create chaos within the country. Therefore, to save our country, we must not buy Japanese goods, which is a bloody path to destroy Japan. To save the country and not become subjugated people, we must rely on ourselves, awaken our conscience, and take the path of using domestic goods. To destroy Japan and avenge our national and personal humiliation, the entire nation must unite and boycott Japanese goods.

(3) If we want to save the country, we must first use domestic goods. (4) The domestic goods movement is an active patriotic movement. (5) Compatriots across the country must unite to promote domestic goods. (6) Down with Japanese imperialism! (7) Long live the Republic of China!

Fifth Batch of Antiquities Transported South 123

Totaling Five Thousand Eight Hundred and Forty-Three Boxes from Four Institutions

Arrived in Shanghai; Guangli Steamer on Sichuan Road Already Dispatched for Transport

The National Palace Museum in Peiping has already transported four batches of antiquities to Shanghai. Now, the fifth batch was transported south from Peiping on the 16th in three trains. Yesterday afternoon, a reporter from the Kuo Wen News Agency visited the warehouse at 26 Rue des Soeurs, Catholic Church Street, in this city to inquire. The reporter met with Xiang Jiajun, the warehouse manager, and obtained the following information.

Five Batches of Antiquities 124

According to Xiang, the five batches of antiquities total 5,843 boxes, transported south on three trains. The station has received a telegram stating that they are expected to arrive in Pukou tonight (the 18th) or tomorrow morning (the 19th). The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has already dispatched the Guangli steamer to transport them. The antiquities belong to four institutions: (1) The Palace Museum (2,412 boxes), (2) The Ministry of Interior Exhibition Hall (3,000 boxes), (3) The Summer Palace of the Peiping Municipal Government (343 boxes), and (4) The Temple Management Office (88 boxes), totaling 5,843 boxes. Including the previous four batches, there are a total of over 13,000 boxes.

Stored on Sichuan Road 125

With the five batches of antiquities being transported south, Yu Tongkui, the Director of General Affairs of the Palace Museum, Director Lu of the Ministry of Interior, and Liu Minjun of the Executive Yuan are escorting them. As for the storage location, the Central Bank has leased a warehouse at 32 Sichuan Road, conveniently located behind the Java-China-Japan Lijn. However, the space is limited, with a maximum capacity of 5,000 boxes, so the remaining boxes will remain at this location (26 Rue des Soeurs). The fifth batch is the last batch, and there will likely be no more antiquities transported south.

Categories of Antiquities 126

Among the five batches of antiquities, from the Palace Museum's perspective, there are still many documents, books, bronzes, and jade objects. The archives have already been completely transported. As for the rumored Jade Buddha of Tuan Cheng, it is unlikely to be in this shipment; otherwise, it would have been mentioned in the telegram. The categories of antiquities from the Ministry of Interior Exhibition Hall are unknown, but based on their usual location, the items displayed in the Wenhua, Wuying, Taihe, Zhonghe, and Baohe Halls in the past are all part of the Exhibition Hall's collection.
