National Goods Weekly Advertising Rates 199

▲ Long lines are calculated at 80 characters per line, with a fee of two yuan per line per issue, minimum 15 lines

▲ Short lines are calculated at 40 characters per line, with a fee of one yuan per line per issue, minimum 30 lines

▲ This publication is published every Thursday

National Goods Forum: National Goods and Tariffs 200

People who are shackled suffer from not being free, everyone knows this. Bad tariffs, layer upon layer of difficulties, this is the suffering of the national goods industry. If this shackle is not removed one day, then the national goods business will have no possibility of development one day. Our government has recently been sparing no effort to promote the national goods business, and is particularly aware of the suffering of the national goods industry. The financial and industrial authorities have also tried to find ways to curb the dumping of foreign goods and reduce the burden on the national goods industry. Recently, the national goods industry has also proposed that the government abolish the transit tax on Chinese-made machine-made goods, and appropriately reduce the import tax on essential raw materials, and increase the import tax on luxury and ordinary goods. It has formally requested the government to adopt it, and the main points are briefly stated as follows: It is found that the collection of a 5% ad valorem tax on machine-made Western-style goods transported and sold domestically, without re-collection, began in the late Qing Dynasty. At that time, it was originally intended to encourage Chinese people to operate new-style industries themselves, so that the Western-style goods they imitated could enjoy the same rights as foreign goods, namely one tax per item, and avoid the suffering of repeated levies. The original intention was extremely thoughtful. However, domestic industry was immature, and commercial power was weak. It was really unable to bear this tax system. After the establishment of the Republic of China, factories in North China repeatedly appealed for its abolition, but it was not approved because there was no way to compensate for the tax revenue. Later, in the thirteenth year of the Republic of China, an additional surcharge of 2.5% was added, making a total of 7.5% with the regular tax, increasing the burden and deepening the suffering. When the National Government moved south and customs autonomy was achieved, various transit taxes similar to likin throughout the country were abolished uniformly, but this transit tax on machine-made Western-style goods was still collected as before, without exemption. The nature of the transit tax is entirely a domestic transit tax, which is actually a type of likin. It should have been abolished at the same time as likin and various tax systems such as the sub-port tax and re-transit tax collected by the customs. Now the sub-port tax has been abolished, but the transit tax on machine-made Western-style goods still exists. In the past, foreign goods transported to the interior were restricted by the sub-port tax, so national goods could barely support themselves. Once the restriction of the foreign goods sub-port tax was lifted, national goods suddenly lost their protection. And this tax system on machine-made Western-style goods, which was originally established to encourage domestic industry, has become an obstacle to the development of domestic industry today. Foreign goods have taken the opportunity to oppress them, and they cannot compete with them. In recent years, factories across the country have been reducing their scale, to the point of suspending operations and closing down. Workers have been reducing their work, to the point of being laid off entirely, which is heard every day. People say that this year is the year of national goods, but it has turned into a year of foreign goods selling well, which is very painful. The government should have been aware of the painful situation of national goods factories. The reason why this tax system was not abolished at the same time as likin was probably because the government was worried about the national treasury revenue and could not give up on it hastily. However, since then, customs duties have been increased twice, and various unified taxes have also been implemented successively, but this transit tax is still delayed and not abolished, causing the national goods industry across the country to decline day by day, which seems to run counter to the government's repeated declarations to protect industry. The Central Political Conference has now resolved to revise the tariff in May of this year. It is believed that this is the best opportunity for our country to relieve the suffering of national industry and commerce and implement a protectionist tariff policy. It is hoped that the government will take into account the imminent danger of national industry, and resolutely abolish this transit tax on machine-made Western-style goods, which is similar to likin, in order to maintain industry and relieve merchants' difficulties. As for the abolition of this tax system, if the revenue from the previous increases in customs duties and the implementation of unified taxes is still insufficient to compensate, it seems that the import tax on foreign goods can be appropriately increased to supplement it. Now that our country's customs sovereignty has been restored, and at this time of revising the tariff again, it coincides with the time when various countries in the world are increasing tariff barriers. It is appropriate to take this opportunity to increase import taxes to alleviate national expenditures. It is proposed to increase the tax rate on imported foreign luxury goods and ordinary goods separately and appropriately. The import tax on raw materials that are lacking in our country's industry and must be supplied from foreign countries is proposed to be appropriately reduced or exempted. For raw materials that our country can manufacture itself without relying on foreign countries, it is also requested to uniformly increase the tax rate, and not be included in the above-mentioned reduction or exemption, in order to conform to the original purpose of protectionist tariffs. In this shift, the national treasury revenue will be surplus, and factories and workers across the country will be rescued. This sincere opinion is the goal of the national goods industry. It is hoped that the government will adopt it as much as possible when deliberating on the tariff, and allow national goods industry groups to send representatives to attend and participate, so as to be consulted. The life and death of the national goods industry depends on this. It is thought that the government authorities, in order to maintain a lifeline for industry, will certainly meet the expectations of our industrial and commercial circles across the country.

National Goods Talk

From the Sound of National Goods to Children's Toys 201

— Huang Jiafu

In industrially backward China, the daily needs of the people have always been supplied by imported goods. As a result, our country's profits are flowing out, the economy is on the verge of bankruptcy, politics are not on track, internal turmoil is frequent, and foreign disasters occur every year. The country is about to perish, which is so painful to say! From now on, if we do not think about saving the country, then so be it. If we want to save the country, then "promoting national goods to recover profits" is indeed a fundamental plan. However, just shouting the slogan "national goods save the country" is useless. We must improve the existing national goods and promote those that do not exist, so that all goods meet the needs of the people and are practical for the people. Then the people will not buy foreign goods but only national goods.

Our country's children's toys are mostly purchased from foreign countries. Although there are no statistics on this loss at present, it must also be a considerable amount. Moreover, children are the future masters of the country, and their toys should be promoted and improved to cater to their psychology and be practical for their play. So that they are happy to buy and use them, cultivate their habit of loving and using national goods, and enlighten their ideas of loving and supporting the country. In this sound of national goods, it is even more necessary. Based on my limited knowledge, I will briefly state the conditions that children's toys should have, as follows:

(1) Must contain educational value.

(2) Must be in accordance with children's hygiene.

(3) Must have beautiful form and solid material.

(4) Must be in accordance with the principle of economy.

(5) Must have multi-faceted activities.

(6) Must have collective use.

(7) Must have no dangerous elements.

(8) Must have no gambling elements.

Goal 202

— Ke Ding'an

In the eyes of ordinary pleasure-seeking friends, the two words "goal" are very unnecessary, because their lives are casual and drifting along, and there is no need for a "goal." But for ordinary sober and active people, whatever they do, they must first set a goal, and then do it according to this goal, so that they can get on track step by step and have a day of success.

What kind of era is it today? We must first recognize it! Foreign aggression cannot be said to be not urgent, and internal strife cannot be said to be not intense. At this critical juncture, what is the most important problem facing us? Of course, there are many, many important problems! Such as air defense facilities, replenishment of armaments, unity of the people, consensus on political views... etc., are all important problems: but I think the most important problem is "using national goods" is relatively important!

"Using national goods" is something that all people across the country can implement uniformly, easily, and is easier to solve than all other problems. Everything in life that is needed can be done in the direction of "using national goods."

However, in our country, where foreign goods are flooding all provinces and villages, and the general public has been assimilated for almost several decades, although they have also performed a "promoting national goods" farce for more than ten years, there are still many who are indifferent. If, back in the fourth year of the Republic, when the Twenty-One Demands were being forced upon us, the people across the country, in accordance with "uniting as one, resisting × goods," had continued until now for more than ten years, I think many historical stains would not have been established, and the tragedies of the September 18th and January 28th incidents would never have happened. What is the reason for this? I think it's not bizarre, nor complicated. It's just that the general public, in the beginning, did not have a clear goal to strive for in "promoting national goods and resisting Japanese goods." If we had really "united as one" and implemented it in the fourth year of the Republic, I think the results now would definitely not be bad!

The fact is unfolding before our eyes. This kind of empty shouting of "promoting national goods and resisting inferior goods" is equal to zero. It not only does not help the actual situation, but also cannot deal with the temporary situation. What else can we do besides standing up and striving for it?

In Shanghai, which is extremely Westernized, we have also suffered the pain of foreign aggression once: but the wealthy people with "millions of dollars" have their good defenses, money. Of course, they will not suffer any pain, but at least it will twitch their brains a little.

The booming sound of cannons and the whirring sound of machine guns have of course become a thing of the past, and our purchase of × goods has also returned to normal! According to the latest report from the customs, taking × goods cotton cloth as an example, in the first and second months, it actually exceeded the large number of more than 840,000 gold units, which is indeed a terrible news that "shakes the heavens and moves the earth, makes ghosts weep and gods cry"!

The creation of this terrible news is undeniably our general public! But our people, none of them are willing to directly admit this crime, which also means that none of them can shirk the burden of this major crime!

Children and National Goods Fashion 203

— Zhang Mengzhao

In cities full of Western-style fashion, it is not easy to promote the prevalence of national goods fashion. So-called modern women, in clothing, food, housing, and transportation, if they do not worship Westernization, they cannot be praised as modern or fashionable. Even if it is ten yuan per foot of foreign silk, they have no worries. They can charm their husbands and lovers, forcing them to drain the pond to get the fish. To hope that they will implement national cloth fashion is simply like asking a tiger for its skin. I think that to promote national goods fashion, we must start with boys and girls. Fathers and brothers should often take their children to national goods companies to arouse their interest in national goods fashion. The two words "national goods" will be deeply imprinted in their minds from an early age. It can be said that there will be unexpected effects. The day before yesterday, I took my four-year-old second son, Changhong, to Sanyou Society to buy clothes. When we went, he was wearing a red crepe Western dress, which was gorgeous and dazzling. But when we put a national cloth Western suit from the national goods company on him, he immediately wanted to abandon the red crepe Western dress and put on the national goods fashion. After we allowed him to change, he was innocent and cheerful, and his spirit was particularly lively. In his little heart, he also seemed very happy. It only cost one yuan, so children and national goods fashion are like electricity and motors!

I think: "The past is like yesterday is dead, the future is like today is born." From now on, we must recognize the goal, and strive to implement the phrase "using national goods." Let us "unite as one" and do it. Everything we need in clothing, food, housing, and transportation should be taken from national goods. Let us no longer act perfunctorily and deceive ourselves. On the one hand, customs imports will decrease day by day, and on the other hand, domestic productivity will increase day by day. Then, those who are arrogant about economic aggression will feel exhausted and eventually perish. At that time: the domestic economy will be prosperous, the people's livelihood will be affluent, there will be no unemployed people, and factories will stand tall. Then, we will not lose the demeanor of the Republic of China, which has thousands of years of history and thousands of years of civilization. This great foundation is completely built on the two words "goal."

National Goods Discussion

New Hopes for China National Goods Company 204

— Wu Zhongfan

China National Goods Company has been established for several months, and its business is booming, which has never been seen in major shopping malls. This shows that the Chinese people love to use national goods, and the company's sincere promotion is sparing no effort. However, after visiting the interior, there are still four shortcomings, which are specifically described below, in order to improve the company.

(1) Accurate Price Marking When entering the building, you can see a piece of white cloth hanging on the wall, on which the prices of various goods are written, starting from a few cents. But when buying, you cannot find the goods of that price, which seems to lose the trust of customers.

(2) Inexpensive Selling Price In recent years, the economy has declined, money has been scarce, and the psychology of ordinary people buying goods is to focus on cheap items. All discount stores in the market are crowded. If the price of goods in the company can be cheaper than other stores, in order to attract customers, the effect of promoting national goods will be greater, and the company's funds will also be easier to circulate.

(3) Expansion of the Shopping Mall The interior location is too small. If customers come in groups of three or five, there will be crowding, which not only reduces the interest of customers, but also easily damages the displayed goods. It is heard that the southern part has been added, and it is hoped that it will be realized as soon as possible.

(4) Printing and Sending National Goods Manuals In recent years, the manufacture of national goods has been changing with each passing day, and the quantity of products has also been gradually increasing. Unfortunately, the Chinese people cannot fully know it, and there are still many who buy foreign goods. If the company can compile a national goods manual, stating the goods and the factories that manufacture them, and give them to customers, although it costs very little, the sales of national goods will be promoted, and the company's business will be more prosperous than it is today.

Two Fabrics Urgently Awaiting Improvement 205

— Chen Jingyu

丨“Self-Strengthening Serge” and “Camel Wool”丨

Regardless of the type of fabric, durability should always be the primary concern; that is, the material should be strong and the color should not fade. Otherwise, it is not a top-quality, authentic product, but rather what is colloquially known as a shoddy product. How can a shoddy product be welcomed by society and expect to sell without any obstruction? However, most of the machine-woven products in China today are plagued by the problem of being shoddy due to being crudely made and not meticulously crafted. The “Self-Strengthening Serge” and “Camel Wool” are prominent examples of this! Now, I am specifically bringing them up for discussion in order to draw the attention of the manufacturers.

New Machine Introduction

Two Domestically Produced Machines 206

— Zhenmu

▲ Adding, Subtracting, Multiplying, and Dividing Calculator 丨丨 This machine was invented and manufactured by Mr. Qian Jinghua of Changshu. It uses the rotation of gears to manually calculate numbers. The machine has a rather small and exquisite appearance, occupying only 2/27 of a cubic foot in volume, making it easy to carry and with a suitable design. The whole machine is divided into three main parts: the real number, the operator number, and the result number. On the two circles of the real and operator numbers, nine digits can be arranged, and the answer machine can have as many as fifteen digits. This type of calculator is already widely popular in foreign countries, and our country is the first to produce it. According to the reporter's observation, the structure of this machine is more advanced than that of foreign products. The advantages include the ability to freely place and correct numbers, the agility of advancing and retreating, the ability to arbitrarily designate and recognize units, the rapid operation of decimals and fractions, the convenience of carrying, and so on.

▲ Panoramic Camera 丨丨 This machine was also invented by Mr. Qian. Ordinary foreign rotating cameras used in photo studios weigh as much as seventeen or eighteen pounds, causing the hands of the person holding it to ache, and the assembly mechanism is also very clumsy. Now, this domestically produced machine, including the lens box and turntable, weighs less than ten pounds, and the shutter light device and the turntable's center of gravity are all very much in line with scientific principles. The suitability of the speed and the accuracy of the distance are also beyond what foreign products can achieve. It is truly an outstanding product of domestic machinery industry and worthy of being advocated and promoted by the Chinese people.

Currently, the domestic goods industry in our country, apart from genuine native products, mostly focuses on efforts in cosmetics and the like. Few people are working on this type of mechanical industry because the effort is doubled and the results are difficult to achieve. Mr. Qian, the inventor of the above two machines, was diligent and thrifty, and began research twenty years ago. He personally operated the machines, and even small screws with a diameter of one hao (a unit of measurement) were manufactured by himself. Therefore, these two machines are truly worthy of being completely domestically produced. However, even after success, the sales have not reached five years, simply because of the lack of publicity, very few Chinese people know about them. And the inventor does not care about fame and fortune, and strives to improve them. Furthermore, most merchants believe in foreign goods that are bulky and inflexible, and despise domestic products. They are willing to buy foreign goods worth one or two thousand yuan, but do not think about buying these domestic products worth six or seven hundred yuan. Therefore, sales have not yet been promoted. It should be known that these two machines are indeed exquisitely made and are not only special products of domestic production, but these two machines have also been registered for patents by the US government, and some have been shipped for sale. I hope that my compatriots will rise up together to advocate their use in order to save our rights and interests.

Page 14

"Self-Strengthening Serge," also known as "Domestic Vienna," originally belonged to a type of cloth. It is said that its structure is silk warp and yarn weft, made by connecting the leftover silk ends from reeling: therefore, there are many small knots on the cloth surface, resembling "pongee," and it looks quite beautiful when new. Unfortunately, the color is terrible. Not to mention that the color fades after a single wash for single-layer clothing, even cotton-padded clothing will change color slightly when exposed to sunlight. Eventually, it deteriorates more and more, looking like old, worn-out things found in the corner of a box, how ugly!

"Camel Wool" is indeed cheaper than foreign goods, and the patterns are no less than foreign goods! However, the effectiveness is far worse; because the texture is very loose, after wearing it for only a few days, the wool fibers will immediately act like cotton, and strands will turn into locks; this alone makes it inelegant. What's more, it will slowly fall off, and the wool fibers will become bare. There is no warmth to speak of!

The above are all major shortcomings! This is not intentional nitpicking, but because the reporter is also one of the supporters of domestic goods, and therefore has to offer well-intentioned advice! I hope that the manufacturers of these two fabrics will quickly remedy the aforementioned shortcomings to achieve perfection! Only then can they compete in the market and compete with foreign goods! If the good advice falls on deaf ears and they stick to their old ways, then when will there be a day for the revitalization of domestic goods?

Domestic Goods News

Domestic Goods Under the Oppression of a False Regime 207

— Zhao Peng

Since the Japanese occupied our Northeast, they have paid great attention to our domestic goods. Goods shipped from Shanghai, Hankou, Tianjin, and other places are considered foreign goods and are subject to heavy taxes. Japanese goods and foreign goods are exempt from taxes, so the price of Japanese goods is 60% lower than that of domestic goods.

The Japanese have repeatedly sent personnel to inspect self-run factories, and they also levy a 25% business tax on their entire business every month. If it is not paid for more than two months, they will be closed down and all property in the store will be confiscated.

In the past, silk satin, homespun cloth, silk fabrics, and cotton fabrics sold well in the Northeast. Now, the Japanese have ordered customs to prohibit imports on the one hand, and on the other hand, they have transported Japanese woolen fabrics, thin silk fabrics, and foreign cloth to the Northeast as much as possible to replace our silk fabrics and cotton fabrics. As a result, our Chinese silk fabrics and cotton fabrics have completely disappeared in the Northeast, and thousands of merchants have closed down one after another. Many southern merchants have closed their businesses and gone south.

My Sister-in-Law's Experience 208

— Yili

We believe that women's clothing is not only related to appearance and hygiene, but also has a profound and significant relationship with the economy of the family.

We also have no hesitation in saying that women's attention to and consideration of clothing are dozens or hundreds of times deeper than men's; because the innate love of beauty can prompt her to study how she can increase her extra beauty. Clothing is certainly the first requirement, and the suitability of tailoring and the selection of clothing materials are a large part of their daily lives. If her father, brothers, or husband is not wealthy, it is easy to develop a kind of depression from being unable to satisfy her desires.

Clever girls and virtuous wives can sometimes restrain their desires and consider the family's finances, and do not often add to their clothes; but such women are indeed relatively few.

Especially young girls, in the golden age like flowers, it would be a pity if they did not have beautiful fashions to wear. In Shanghai or the inland areas near Shanghai, a generation of girls have suffered significant losses and serious lessons because of clothing, which is already very obvious. Their shortcomings are because their understanding of fashion is not yet clear. First, they cannot tailor themselves; second, they cannot create themselves; third, they do not understand how to choose clothing materials. They only know to consult tailors, only know to buy expensive imported goods, and only know to imitate the styles created by others. It is naturally very uneconomical and inconvenient to buy imported goods and consult tailors for every piece of clothing.

My brother recently married a clever sister-in-law. She is indeed beautiful, but she cannot be considered very beautiful. The clothes she wears are not only fashionable, but also often have new styles. Many relatives and friends praised her as a fashion expert. I do not quite believe that my brother has so much money to provide her to spend on clothing, nor have I ever seen tailors come to our house to deliver new clothes to her.

As we became more familiar, I brought up this doubt and asked her in very appropriate words, and carefully investigated her, and found out that every night, she was hiding in her room, carefully sewing clothes herself, so she was able to use her intelligence to create various different styles of fashion.

She also told me: The beauty of women's clothing does not depend entirely on the clothing material, but on whether the tailoring is suitable. Often general clothing materials, the excess scraps, (whether they are leftover from the width or the remaining length,) are carefully kept. Sometimes they can also be used when tailoring other clothes. Imported goods are too expensive, so naturally choose domestic goods. For example: for summer clothing materials now, double crepe and georgette, there are many products from domestic manufacturers such as the Meya Silk Weaving Factory; and new patterns are emerging one after another. As long as you choose for yourself, whichever pattern is suitable for your environment, suitable for your age, self-tailoring and skin color, buy it and tailor it yourself, then you have it.

In Shanghai now, the common practice is that the money to buy a piece of clothing material may not be very expensive (unless you buy luxurious imported goods), but the tailoring fee is very high; or even more expensive than the clothing material. That will affect the family's finances.

Therefore, to wear fashionable clothes, the best thing to do is to learn how to tailor first; otherwise, at a minimum, you must buy domestic goods, and domestic silk crepe from the Continental Commercial Market China National Goods Company is the most reliable, and the price is the most suitable. According to my sister-in-law's experience, buying imported georgette to make a cheongsam, if you ask a tailor to tailor it, and buying Meya factory georgette and tailoring it yourself, the money used is a ratio of three to one; in other words, if you buy foreign clothing material and do not tailor it yourself, you can only wear one piece. If you buy domestic clothing material and tailor it yourself with the same amount of money, you can wear three pieces, is this not very economical?

The styles of fashion change very quickly. If you often want to wear fashionable clothes, it is very uneconomical; rather than spending a sum of money to only wear one piece, why not wear three pieces?

— Sun Choucheng

On Domestic Goods Trademarks 211

— Manbin

A trademark is a sign of a commodity. If a commodity has credit, then people will have no doubt about buying goods at the sight of the trademark. The common saying old brand means that the brand has supreme value. In the past, trademarks in our country did not go beyond the names of Tianguan, Longevity Star, Harmony, Eight Immortals, Four Joys, Auspicious, and Ruyi, which were passed down layer by layer and were easy to confuse. Recently, the domestic goods industry has been developing day by day, and domestic products are also increasing day by day. Attention is also being paid to the exclusive use of trademarks. The government has set up a special bureau to be in charge of it, and factories regard commodities as the sole life of the entire factory. Therefore, the issue of trademarks has aroused unanimous attention in society and is felt to be a very interesting issue. In terms of the characteristics of trademarks, there are all kinds of colors and strange shapes, which are the best of ingenuity. In my opinion, the most important thing about a trademark is that it is simple and easy to remember. The triangle of Three Friends and the three stars of China are so simple and concise. Taking materials and homophony is also full of fun. The butterfly of Invincible and the five geese of Wuhe are examples of this. Taking animals as materials, there are standing cranes and flying tigers, flying horses, and dog heads. Taking plants as materials, there are ink chrysanthemums and evergreens. There are goddesses like Chang'e, and ghosts like Zhong Kui, everything is available, and the efforts of the factory authorities are so commendable and admirable. However, trademarks are dead objects, and commodities are also inactive. If you want commodities to be sold, you must rely entirely on the refinement of manufacturing and have credit. If you do not produce crudely, do not cut corners, then the reputation will get better and better, and any trademark can spread without legs.

Publicity should have practical work, and jointly seek industrial development. At a minimum, the following basic conditions should be met: (1) Break the inferiority of superstitious foreign goods, (2) Develop the habit of loving and using domestic goods. Now, the fierce and stubborn Japanese imperialists have seized our land and are taking further steps to destroy our nation. If we want to avenge our shame and revitalize the national fortune, we must permanently break off economic relations with Japan and promote domestic goods consistently. County government representative Shen Mengyang gave a detailed account of the annual excess imports. County Party representative Yang Zaoshi said that the previous promotion of domestic goods movement in Pinghu was mostly done in words or verbally, which was abstract. This time, inviting domestic goods factories in Shanghai and Hangzhou to bring their products for display was unprecedented and practical. County backbone team representative Fan Liming gave a speech, asking vendors to abandon foreign goods and sell domestic goods in the future, and asking producers to study carefully so that domestic goods can become better and better and surpass imported goods. Finally, Domestic Goods Federation representative Ma Jisheng gave a reply on behalf of all manufacturers, which was a grand occasion at the time.

Interview Notes

Mr. Hu Xiyuan 212

— Yueyun

Anyone who runs a real business is worthy of admiration, especially in our country where production is backward.

To run a real business, you must have the following conditions in order to achieve considerable success. What are those conditions? They are: (1) Endurance of labor and hardship. (2) Willingness to sacrifice. (3) Strong capital. (4) Utmost impartiality and selflessness. (5) Broad vision.

Because they can endure labor and hardship, they can safely cross the turbulent waves when they encounter them. Because they are willing to sacrifice, they still strive and fight hard when they clearly know they will lose money, arousing the belief of ordinary people. With strong capital, they can continue to compete with foreign goods. With the spirit of utmost impartiality and selflessness, they can share the joys and sorrows with others. With a broad vision, they will not produce crudely and seek temporary benefits. Those who run real businesses in our country who can meet these conditions will definitely succeed.

Mr. Hu Xiyuan's China Yaopuer Electric Appliance Factory, I heard that since its opening, it has gone through many storms, and the dumping of foreign goods and the infighting of the same industry have been able to pass smoothly. This cannot but be attributed to Mr. Hu's perseverance.

Because the China Yaopuer Electric Appliance Factory has a considerable position in the current domestic goods industry, and at the same time, I heard friendly rumors, I also have a considerable understanding of this Mr. Hu, so I resolutely went to visit him. Mr. Hu's kind appearance, sincere attitude, and told me the history of China Yaopuer Electric Appliance Factory in detail, such as opening in 1925, adding from tens of thousands of capital to one hundred thousand, then to two hundred thousand, three hundred thousand, and now it is five hundred thousand. From ordinary houses of three rooms and two sides, it has expanded to buying land and building new-style factory buildings for the glass department, the light bulb department, and the motor department. Although it has experienced several storms in the meantime, it has always been determined to remain calm and deal with them by chance. He had no arrogance, nor did he have any words of sigh, always smiling very kindly.

He led me to visit the glass department, where the furnace was blazing, and dozens of workers were picking materials, blowing bubbles, and working very quickly. When I arrived at the light bulb department, there were about two hundred male and female workers. Here, except for the rattling of the machines, it was almost silent. Some were installing hooks, some were stretching silk, and some were exhausting air, all of which were divided into labor and cooperation. Finally, I went to the motor department on Poyang Road in Yangshupu. There, the fields were surrounded by fields and the air was very good. There were about one hundred workers, divided into several groups: fitter, lathe worker, painter, assembler, etc. The work was very intense, and it turned out that the fan was about to be in season.

After returning from the visit, I gave Mr. Hu a two-word comment in my opinion, which is "sincere." For the Yaopuer Electric Appliance Factory, there are sixteen words to evaluate it, which are "talented people are gathered. The equipment is complete. Work hard to manufacture. Products are of high quality."

Ashamed Chinese Movie Stars 213

— Jingcun

In the film supplement of a certain Japanese newspaper last month, there was a segment about Clara Bow's life in Europe. I do not avoid the crime of plagiarism and copy it once.

Clara Bow's Patriotic Enthusiasm

"Clara Bow and her husband have been traveling in Europe for more than a month now. According to news from Europe, since Clara Bow arrived in Europe, she has not bought any items for her daily use except for food, not even an underwear. When it is absolutely necessary, she must also buy American products from the store. Clara Bow made many clothes in the United States before she set off, worth about eight thousand gold yuan, so although she changes the style of her clothes every day in Paris, she still does not feel a lack. Paris merchants originally expected to do good business this time when Clara Bow arrived in Europe, but unexpectedly, Clara Bow was determined not to buy anything but American goods. Generally, people felt unexpected. However, French merchants do not resent Clara Bow's patriotism because they have not done good business, and they respect Clara Bow very much." After reading this news, I couldn't help but feel ashamed. Clara Bow is a world-famous movie star. Although she earned a lot of money from foreigners in her home country, this time when she went to Europe, the merchants in Paris were hoping to earn some decoration expenses from her, but they were disappointed. Clara Bow did not buy even an underwear, let alone other jewelry and new clothes, but French merchants did not resent her for not being able to do business with her, but respected her for not forgetting to buy domestic goods even after becoming a star.

Why do I feel ashamed after reading this news? Think about it, has any Chinese movie star won world honors? Despite the flattery of boring writers, their art and their words and deeds do not seem to arouse our respect and admiration. I am an outsider to the art of film, so I will not discuss how the film saves the country, we have not yet seen it, but there are full-page advertisements in newspapers every day, and movie stars personally sign to promote foreign goods and prove foreign goods. Movie stars are worthy of being loyal servants to foreign merchants, using foreign goods themselves, and also advising ordinary people to use foreign goods. I think, if Clara Bow came to Shanghai and saw this phenomenon, she would definitely say "Bah, is this called a star?" I think Chinese stars are really ashamed!

Astounding Absurdities 214

— Qin Shouou

I am a tumbler that grew up in the Great China Domestic Goods Toy Factory. My father is also Chinese, and my mother is also Chinese. In summary, I am indeed an unadulterated descendant of the Yellow Emperor: However, less than half a month after I grew up completely in the factory, our boss sent me and my four or five hundred brothers to a tall company with seven or eight floors, and let us rest in a large glass cabinet.

After a few days, a team of tumblers that looked similar to us suddenly came. I secretly paid attention to their backs, and saw that the four characters "China National Goods" were also engraved. I thought they were always our compatriots, so I went over to greet them, but unexpectedly they couldn't understand my words, and I couldn't understand a single word they said either. The most surprising thing to me was that what they said was neither Cantonese nor Hokkien, but sounded somewhat like Japanese.

Later, one of them who could speak Chinese secretly told me; "To be honest, we all came from Japan. Unexpectedly, when we arrived in Shanghai, merchants of your country engraved the four characters "China National Goods" on our backs, and I don't even know why?"

After listening to his words, I was in a daze and confused when a customer happened to come outside. The clerk was busy greeting him with a smile.

"Do you want to buy domestic toys? Very good, this is a genuine domestic product!" The customer first said that he wanted to buy a domestic tumbler, and the clerk agreed non-stop, but he reached in and deliberately picked a fake domestic product from Japan.

"Sir, look how good this is, and the price is cheap, half the price of the other one!" The clerk said with a burst of flattery, and the customer was fooled, and paid the money very satisfied and left with the fake domestic product.

"Hee hee...". The clerk was overjoyed and laughed out loud. I was full of fire with hatred, but unfortunately I couldn't move my hands, otherwise I would have given him a slap in the face.

Ministry of Education Requests Increased Funding from the Ministry of Finance Due to Financial Strain 219

▲ Hoping for Equal Treatment with Other Ministries

The original budget for the Ministry of Education was 42,000 yuan per month. After the national crisis, the Ministry of Finance allocated 21,000 yuan. After deducting 2,500 yuan for the Compilation and Translation Bureau, the actual amount received was 18,500 yuan. In the past, the Ministry relied on the relief from the Zhejiang Province's poppy tax. Since the poppy tax can no longer be paid as usual, difficulties have been felt. The Ministry of Education, considering that the majority of other ministries have already received 70% or more of their allocated funds, while the Ministry of Education has only received 50%, and the actual expenditure, even after reductions due to the national crisis, is still above 70% of the original budget, has specially requested the Ministry of Finance to follow the precedent of other ministries and provide 70% of the Ministry of Education's funding starting from May, in order to alleviate the situation.

Local News

Tongji University to Add a Higher Vocational School 220

▲ Utilizing the Labor University's Engineering College

▲ Starting with a Pilot Mechanical Engineering Department

丨Northwest Agricultural and Forestry College to Not Enroll Students During Summer Vacation丨

The equipment of the Labor University's factories and classrooms related to the Engineering College was transferred to Tongji University by the Ministry of Education the other day. It is now heard that Tongji University has decided to utilize the school's mechanical engineering talent after the summer vacation, using the existing facilities of the Labor University to establish a higher vocational school. A pilot mechanical engineering department will be launched first, and formal enrollment will begin after the summer vacation. As for the Labor University's agricultural college and farm equipment, they have been allocated to the preparatory committee of the Northwest Agricultural and Forestry College. The Labor University's regular monthly expenses of 50,000 yuan will be managed by the Northwest Agricultural College preparatory committee starting this month. The Ministry of Education has already informed the Ministry of Finance of this on the 16th. It is said that the Northwest Agricultural and Forestry College preparatory committee will actively prepare throughout this year, but there will be no enrollment after the summer vacation. Enrollment of new students is expected to begin in the spring of next year.

Executive Directors of the Secondary School Teachers' Association

Opposing the Soviet Union's Sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway 221

▲ Decision to Send Telegrams Nationwide to Pay Attention to the Situation in North China

The Shanghai Secondary School Teachers' Association held its fifth executive directors' meeting at its headquarters yesterday afternoon at 3 PM. Those in attendance were Sheng Xugong, Xu Zexiang, Li Yongzhong, Shen Zuru, Wu Baoyue, Liu Zirun, Cheng Daomin, Chen Shizhong, Liao Zhaojun, and Xue Daren. Sheng Xugong presided over the meeting, and Xu Zexiang recorded the minutes. (1) Regarding the motion to establish a Secondary Education Research Association, which was referred by the board of directors, it was decided to task the academic division with convening the meeting within one week. (2) Regarding the motion to oppose the Soviet Union's sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway, it was decided to approve the principles, and: 1. A telegram will be sent to the government to protest to the Soviet Union; 2. A telegram will be sent to the ambassador to the Soviet Union to convey the opposition of the people of this country; 3. A telegram will be sent to the Soviet government expressing opposition; 4. A telegram will be sent to our country's representative to the League of Nations to raise opposition in the League of Nations; 5. A telegram will be sent to the League of Nations Secretariat requesting it to stop the sale; 6. Representatives will be sent to the Russian Embassy in China with official letters to express opposition. The documentation division will handle the above cases. (3) Regarding the motion for the association to hold meetings once a week, it was decided to approve it, and it was decided that meetings will be held promptly at 9 AM every Sunday. (4) Regarding the motion on how the association should respond to the fall of the Northeast and the precarious situation in Tianjin and Beijing, it was decided that: 1. A telegram will be sent to national civil society groups urging them to pay attention to the seriousness of the situation in North China; 2. An emergency temporary board meeting will be convened at 8 AM on the 21st of this month to discuss rescue measures. (5) Regarding the motion to pass the detailed rules of the Cultural Introduction Committee, it was decided to pass it with revisions.

Cai Yuanpei Discusses the Feasibility of Independent Education Funding 222

Regarding independent education funding, Zheng Hongnian, when he was Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, drafted a method that was discussed and decided upon by the Executive Yuan's council, and then handed over to Jia Shiyi of the Ministry of Finance and Duan Xipeng of the Ministry of Education to jointly draft a method and submit it for review. However, due to the outbreak of the Shanghai Battle, it was shelved. Now, the Shanghai University Teachers' Association believes that reorganizing education requires making independent education funding the current urgent task, so it has specially initiated the organization of a committee to protect independent education funding, dedicated to this matter. According to Cai Yuanpei, a member of the committee, protecting independent education funding was originally one of the Chinese Nationalist Party's policies, and it was decided to allocate the Boxer Indemnity as education funding. Currently, the universities in North China still use the Boxer Indemnity as part of their education funding. The new Minister of Education, Mr. Wang Xueting, has always paid close attention to independent education funding. If there is a concrete method for this matter, it seems that it will not be difficult to see it realized.

Shanghai Education Bureau Destroys Banned Books 224

The Shanghai Education Bureau recently destroyed a considerable number of banned books. It is reported that the Bureau confiscated and destroyed the following from various bookstores: one copy of "Black Love" and "Youth" (original title) from Modern Bookstore, along with all printing plates; thirty-one copies of "Epoch-Making Transformation," along with printing plates; two hundred and seven copies of "The Collected Works of My Late Mother," along with printing plates comprising one hundred and forty-one pages; "Modern Literature Reader," along with printing plates comprising sixty-one pages; one hundred and twenty-three copies of "Youth Book," along with printing plates comprising seventy-two pages; printing plates from pages two hundred and sixteen to two hundred and seventeen of "Ten Years of Creation"; thirty-six copies of "Blood Sacrifice" from Guanghua Bookstore, along with printing plates; one hundred and seventy-four copies of "The Third Period" from Hufeng Bookstore, along with printing plates; one thousand and fifty-one copies of "Little People's Book: The Eastern and Western Han Dynasties," five hundred and fifty-seven copies of "The Romance of the Seven Kingdoms," two hundred and ninety-seven copies of "Miss Huang," along with printing plates comprising two hundred and twenty pages; three thousand four hundred and seventy-one copies of "Little People's Book: Journey to the West" from Guangji Bookstore, printing plates for "Diao Liu's Renaming to Avenge Her Master," comprising two hundred and forty pages; twenty-seven copies of "New Taixing" from Xin Taixing Company; and eighty-seven copies of "New Creation," Volume 1, Issues 1-6, from Taidong Bookstore, all of which were destroyed successively.

Shanghai Education Bureau Notifies Graduation Examination Dates 225

The Shanghai Education Bureau issued a directive yesterday to municipal and registered private primary, junior, and senior high schools, stating: "Regarding the graduation examinations for students in the primary, junior, and senior high school general programs for the second semester of the 21st year, the methods have been determined and promulgated. The dates for the examinations have now been decided: junior and senior high schools will be held on June 15, 16, and 17 for three days; primary schools will be held on June 19 and 20 for two days. Each school must conduct its own graduation examinations by the end of May, and student academic and conduct report cards must be submitted to the Bureau no later than June 10. The locations for the examinations will be announced separately after they are selected. This directive is issued for your information."

The Last Telegram Received by Jiaotong University Before the Fall of Tangshan 227

▲ 5 PM Last Saturday

▲ No News Since Then

The situation in Tangshan after its fall is unclear. The National Jiaotong University in Shanghai has an engineering college located there. After the outbreak of the fighting in eastern Luan, all the students began evacuating to Shanghai last month. All the school equipment was also shipped to Tianjin by the college's president, Sun Hongzhe. Only a few staff members and laborers were left behind in Tangshan to guard the premises. However, the college had a radio station that could communicate with the Shanghai campus daily, so the situation there was very clear. However, after 5 PM last Saturday, the college's radio station suddenly went silent. The university authorities made several attempts to contact them, but were unable to. Although telegrams were also sent to the Tangshan train station via the railway telegraph line in an attempt to inquire about the college's situation, there was no reply. As a result, the situation there is impossible to ascertain. The telegram sent at 5 PM last Saturday stated that the situation there was already very chaotic, with unfavorable news from the front lines pouring in like snowflakes. The local garrison troops were retreating without fighting. Many of the major factories in the area owned by Chinese were tragically bombed by Japanese planes. However, the college was fortunately still safe. From this observation, the situation in Tangshan was already extremely dangerous last Saturday afternoon, and the area fell that evening. Because the college had a radio station, the Japanese army must have immediately dispatched a team to guard it. The silence of the college's radio station may be due to the Japanese army's tyrannical obstruction.

▲ Shanghai Education Bureau Ordered to Prepare

The Shanghai Education Bureau received an order from the Municipal Government yesterday, stating that, according to an order from the Examination Yuan, higher and general qualification examinations should be held in each province and city before the higher examinations are held, and the Examination Committee is authorized to consult with the former committee. The Bureau was ordered to comply with the order, promptly determine a date, and hold the examinations within the specified time limit. After receiving the order, it is said that the Bureau has begun preparations. The examination date is expected to be in early July. Minsheng Women's School to Establish a Summer School 231

Minsheng Women's School, located at the intersection of Avenue Joffre in the French Concession, has specially hired Mr. Yu Lisan, a graduate of Jiaotong University, Mr. Wu Xihui, a teacher at Taihu Middle School, as well as Mr. Wang Zhen and Hu Shaobai, the school's academic directors, to establish a tutoring school for Chinese, English, and mathematics during the summer vacation, divided into three sections: junior, senior, and first-year junior high school. Preparations are currently underway, and classes are scheduled to begin in early July. It is reported that students from other schools can also register for admission.

Fourth Central School Sports Federation

Track and Field Meet 238

Notes for Participating Schools

The Track and Field Meet organized by the Fourth Central School Sports Federation will be held tomorrow and the day after at the China Athletic Field. All the competition matters have been prepared. The Standing Committee of the Federation has now issued six notes for participating schools, which should be paid special attention to:

(1) Today from 2 PM to 4 PM, please send representatives from each school to the National Sports Promotion Association to pick up the number cloths, badges, and program books.

(2) On the opening day, all athletes must bring their school flags and enter the stadium in formation before 1 PM. All students of member schools are exempt from admission fees but must come with the team; otherwise, they must purchase tickets.

(3) The athlete's number cloth must be sewn on both the front and back of the chest (not sewn elsewhere) and must be sewn tightly at all four corners or fastened with pins. Violators will not be allowed to participate.

(4) The opening ceremony will be held tomorrow at 1:30 PM. The order of school arrangement is as follows: (1) Organizing Committee, (2) Minli Middle School, (3) Daxia Affiliated Middle School, (4) Fudan Shizhong, (5) Fudan Affiliated Middle School, (6) Jinan Affiliated Middle School, (7) Guanghua Affiliated Middle School, (8) Shanghai Middle School, (9) Hujiang Affiliated Middle School. Each school should be arranged in the following order: A. School Flag, B. Coach, C. Female Athletes, D. Male Athletes, all in two rows.

(5) Every time an event is held, there will be three announcements. At the time of the first announcement, each competitor may enter the stadium to warm up their muscles. At the time of the third announcement, all competitors must gather at the location of the event and wait quietly for the roll call. Those who do not arrive will be considered to have forfeited.

(6) Athletes from each school are not allowed to enter the stadium outside of the competition time and are not allowed to stay in the stadium after the competition is over.

(7) All sports equipment is generously provided by the Lao Ximen Standard Sports Equipment Company, but each school can also bring its own, as long as it is approved by the referee.

He stated that difficulties were encountered in terms of economy and time, making it difficult to implement. However, regarding the two proposals raised by Shen Guoquan, "During the season of a certain sport, official team members of schools affiliated with this association are not allowed to participate in any external leagues," it was resolved that the various competitions scheduled by this association should not be postponed due to external competitions (except for international or charitable competitions).

(4) Organized a constitution revision committee, nominating Guanghua, Jiaotong, Daxia, Jinan, and Chizhi universities, with Jiaotong University convening the committee.

Forward US Dollar Rises Sharply, Gold Price Drops by 11.7 Yuan 242

Those who rushed in previously yesterday sold off one after another

The gold market experienced a sharp rise the day before yesterday, but failed to break through the 1,000 mark, causing uncertainty. Unexpectedly, yesterday morning, the forward US dollar rose by more than one cent, and those who entered the market the day before yesterday sold off one after another. The gross price immediately dropped to 82.3 yuan. Major players such as Qian Changxiang, Chunyuan, Yonghong, Lifu, and Changchang, as well as Qingfa, Yongchang Sheng, Yongdai, and a certain Mr. Wu, all sold off, causing further downstream pressure. After opening, the price rose and fell with the exchange rate. The domestic price once tightened, and the gold price was once hyped up to 83.5 yuan. However, Ruixing, acting for Joe Chivu, sold aggressively, and Fuchang and others also sold off fiercely, resulting in a decline. However, in comparison, the bulls were still more advantageous. The revealed price for today is slightly distant, so there is a lack of bulls in the swap market. The price for this month is 60 yuan higher, and the swap price for June and July is 13 yuan lower, which may be due to bookkeeping. There were no special changes in half a day, and the market situation was the opposite of the day before yesterday. The industry suddenly sold US dollars, and there were still many bidders for future delivery, so the process was still smooth. Here is a record of the market situation for the first half of the day.

The morning opening was 976.5 yuan, which was 12 yuan lower than the previous close. The price of goods opened at the same price. The exchange market opened with the British exchange rate at 1 shilling 2 pence 6875, and the US exchange rate at 24.0625 yuan. At first, the market was still stable. After hovering, Tongfeng, Hengbingxing, and Hengyu all took delivery. Fuchang, Yuansheng, and Yong also entered. Although it was able to rise, it was because Huabi was eating US dollars for June at 0625, and half a yuan for August as well. It rose to 80 yuan. Ruixing, Hengyu, Daxing, and Yong all sold, and the trend was still low. HSBC stuffed out US dollars for August at 4375. Before long, Bingxing suddenly sold off US dollars for September at 6875, and the price fell to 74.8 yuan. Pan Gen ate 75 for September, and the market stabilized. After entering the market, all the banks wanted this price. Qingfa, Yong, Fuchang, and Fuyu all entered, and it rose to 9.4 yuan. The HSBC listing rose 25 for British currency and 125 for US currency. At this time, the market hovered around 8 yuan. HSBC continuously ate US dollars for June at 125. Fuchang, Bingxing, Zhifeng, Yongheng, Yuchangyu, and others all entered the market together. Huabi also grabbed US dollars for August at 5625, and it rose to over 82 yuan. After entering the market, the domestic price once tightened. US dollars for August at 4375 were wanted by all the banks. Shunli came up to buy. It was once hyped up to 83.5 yuan. Zhifeng, Yongzhaofengchang took the opportunity to sell, but because Mitsui was grabbing US dollars for August at 375, it was still able to stand at around 2 yuan. However, with a large number of sellers, the trend was still downward. Datong sold half a yuan for August to Huabi. Ruixing, Fuchang, and Zhaofengchang all sold, and it retreated to within 80 yuan. Yuanxingyong also came on the scene to sell, and it retreated further to within 7 yuan. Fuchang, Ruixing, Dafa, and Yong repeatedly sold aggressively, and it dropped to 5.5 yuan. The price of goods was picked up, pulling up by more than 2 yuan. However, with the exchange market hardening, US dollars for August at 5625 were difficult to sell again, and it retreated to 5 yuan. Huabi ate 5625 for August. Hengyu, Yuanmao, and Yong entered at 8.6 yuan. Shunli aggressively sold, and it was 5.1 yuan. Before long, the noon closing was 976.8 yuan, and the price of goods was the same. It was found that the highest price in the half-day was 983.5 yuan, and the lowest price was 974.8 yuan, with a fluctuation of 8.7 yuan. As a result, it fell back 11.7 yuan compared to the previous close.

The revealed price was calculated at 23.625 yuan due to HSBC's US dollar listing rising by 125, totaling 1,015.87 yuan. Based on the closing price, it was about 39 yuan lower, which was 6 yuan more than the previous close. The price for registration this month was 1,009 yuan, 989 yuan for June, and 977 yuan for July. The afternoon subsidy was 1,009 yuan. The price for this month was calculated to be 60 yuan higher, but there were no formal transactions. There were still few swap deals, because the revealed price was far away, resulting in a lack of long positions. (The price of goods for May and June was over 21.5 yuan). For June and July, Tongfenheng offered to subsidize Qian Changxiang 5,516 lots, with a subsidy of 13 yuan, which may be a bookkeeping transaction. The bidding price in the market was generally 14 or 15 yuan. There were still 2,492 lots left for May, and 7,651 lots for June. The short positions were Tongfenheng Shenkang Hengyu Daxingyong Hengxing, and the long positions were Qian Changxiang Runchangyong Dadecheng, etc.

The market transaction changed to oversupply. In summary, Ruixing (acting for Joe Chivu), Fuchang, Zhaofengchang, Yuanxingyong, Dafa Yongshunli, etc. all sold. Tongfenheng Hengxing Fuyu Runchangyu Wanxing Hengyu, etc. all entered. In the gross market, Qian Changxiang Chunyuan Yonghong Lifu Changchang Shengyong Qingfa Yong (heard acting for a certain Mr. Wu) all sold. Bingxing Zhifengyong first entered and then exited. The Dalian gang Wanxing entered more than 200. Shunli exited. The Guangdong gang had little entry or exit. US Dollar Rises, British and US Exchange Rates Both Harden 243

丨The gold industry suddenly sold off and exited more than 200,000丨

According to foreign telegrams yesterday, the London large contract for both near and far dates fell by 0625, the British currency against the US currency fell by one-third of 125, and the US currency against the British currency fell by a small quarter. The near-term British exchange rate opened at 1 shilling 2 pence 6875, which was 25 harder than the previous close. The New York silver price rose 25, and the forward silver price actually rose by more than one cent. The private telegram then added one cent. US cotton fell slightly. The opening selling price of the near-term US exchange rate was 24.0625 yuan, which was 25 harder than the previous close. After opening, it twice turned from tight to loose. The HSBC listing rose 25 for shillings and 125 for US currency. The announcement was still flat. The process fluctuated, and the result seemed hard. By noon, the near-term selling price was 1 shilling 2 pence 75, which was 3125 harder than the previous close. The US exchange rate was 24.0625 yuan, which was 25 harder than the previous close. Banks were grabbing more than they were stuffing. Huabi, HSBC, Mitsui, and Meifeng were on the buying side. The gold industry was stuffing, but not much, about 200,000. In addition, they were seeing grabbing and stuffing from time to time, and the trend was still flat. Here is a record of the bank transactions for the first half of the day.

Silk and Tea, Early Silkworms in Suzhou and Zhejiang Affected by Thunderstorms 256

(Sheng County) Farmers in the north and south cities and villages are unable to raise silkworms this year, and they all borrow money to buy seeds. Most of them raise foreign species. In villages such as Sanjie, Chongren, Ganlin, Houshan, and Huatang, the amount of feeding is relatively smooth. The weather is mild, and there are instructors running around to guide them. The silkworm ants are developing healthily, and the early gangs have entered the big sleep. However, in the Qingshuitang Ma'ao Shangjiang Rencun area, some people still raise native species, which are now flourishing with leaves. However, due to continuous thunderstorms and strong winds, the silkworm farmers cannot dry the leaves in time, causing the native silkworms to develop diseases such as yellow leakage. The foreign silkworms are also sluggish in eating leaves and have uneven sleep heads due to sudden cold and heat. The instructors are running around to rescue them and are trying to isolate them to avoid infection.

(Yangzhong) The farmers in the four villages are all raising foreign species this year, borrowing money. Some people hatch native species due to lack of borrowing channels, resulting in inconsistent silkworm flood times. The early native silkworms have now been sleeping three times and have enough leaves. The foreign silkworms are sleeping three times and releasing leaves. The silkworm ants are developing well. Unexpectedly, there have been repeated thunderstorms, strong winds, rain, and hail in the past two days. The native early silkworms in the coastal sands have changed, and they have abdominal diarrhea due to eating rain leaves, and they have white zombie disease due to uneven cold and heat. Foreign silkworms are also delaying sleep and eating leaves slowly. Silkworm farmers are all holding hidden worries. The supply of mulberry leaves exceeds the demand, and there is still no market price.

A Look at the Qifu Tea Market

New Tea Production with Tender Heads 258

The new black tea from the four villages of Qifu has been opened by mountain households for picking and drying for more than ten days. However, due to the cold weather, the tea body cannot be enlarged in order, and the leaf quality is very tender. According to tea masters, this year's tea leaves are produced thinly and tenderly. Most of those who pick and make them on sunny days have excellent color, aroma, and taste. However, the output is less than last year because the tea is tender and cannot be picked out.

Tea Households Feel Pain from Low Prices 259

This year, the Qifu tea houses suffered a major loss last year, and the prices to the mountains were uniformly lowered. The top character high village goods in Qixi only sold for 65 or 66 yuan, and the Qicheng and Nanlu tea only sold for 54 or 55 yuan, a drop of 40 or 50 yuan per dan compared to 120 or 130 yuan for Qixi goods last year and 80 or 90 yuan for Qinan goods. The household's annual cost of living, which relies on tea prices, has been reduced by half this year. The half price they get, after deducting labor, food, and miscellaneous expenses, is very little left. This year, the Qifu tea households have suffered another disaster.

Tea Warehouses Carefully Release Exchanges 260

This year, the warehouse owners are afraid of the discount of the Qishang last year, and the scope of the release of funds has been greatly reduced. They visually inspect the credit of the owners of the company. Each company is limited to releasing up to 4,000. As of now, the tea silver released by each warehouse is only 800,000 yuan in total, which is 2.2 million yuan less than last year. Considering the interests of the warehouse owners themselves, this tightening policy also shows the necessary steps to know the danger.

Tea Number Decreases by Ninety-Five 261

This year, the original numbers were hit by the low tea market last year. Most of the capital was lost, and new sources of funds were not comfortable. Although the tea warehouses have a relief of 4,000 loans, the amount is minimal. According to the latest survey, there are only 259 tea numbers in the three counties of Qifu, which is a decrease of 95 compared to last year. Moreover, they are all short of capital and cannot expand as widely as in previous years, and import as much tea as possible.

The Cost of New Tea is Not Light 262

In recent years, the price of Qifu tea has continued to rise. The tea merchants have no standards and have been fighting to raise the price. This year's cost is still not light. According to the top-character raw tea bought by each number, the price is 60 yuan per dan. The cost of making finished boxes is about 200 yuan. The cost of purchasing Qinggong tea at a price of 200 yuan per tael, and making one catty of dry tea from three catties, is about 300 yuan per dan. Judging from the current tea market in Shanghai, the stored red is priced from 80 taels to 30 taels per dan. Then the new tea, which requires 200 to 300 yuan per dan, cannot avoid loss again.
